## 1. 🏗️ Architecture Decision: TypeScript/Node.js (Confirmed)

**Decision:** **Full-Stack TypeScript** with process isolation via `worker_threads` + `child_process`.

**Rationale:**
| Factor | TypeScript | Go/Java |
|--------|------------|---------|
| MCP SDK Native | ✅ Official @modelcontextprotocol/sdk | ❌ Requires bindings |
| Dashboard Unity | ✅ Shared types (packages/types) | ❌ API contract overhead |
| Ecosystem | ✅ All AI tools TS-first | ❌ Integration friction |
| Development Speed | ✅ Rapid iteration | ❌ Compile/deploy cycles |
| Plugin System | ✅ Dynamic imports | ❌ Static typing limits |

**Stability Strategy:**
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    MAIN PROCESS (Control Plane)              │
│  Express + tRPC + WebSocket + Event Bus + Registry State    │
└──────────────┬──────────────────────────────┬───────────────┘
               │                              │
    ┌──────────▼──────────┐      ┌───────────▼────────────┐
    │   WORKER THREADS    │      │   CHILD PROCESSES      │
    │   (Agent Logic)     │      │   (CLI/MCP Servers)    │
    │  • Isolated v8 ctx  │      │  • Crash containment   │
    │  • Model inference  │      │  • stdio/SSE bridges   │
    │  • Planning/ranking │      │  • Auto-restart logic  │
    └─────────────────────┘      └────────────────────────┘
```

## 3. 💻 Core Implementation

### 3.1 Provider Fallback Engine (`packages/core/src/services/ProviderFallbackService.ts`)

```typescript
// packages/core/src/services/ProviderFallbackService.ts
import { EventEmitter } from 'events';
import { ModelProvider, ModelConfig, QuotaStatus } from '../types/providers';
import { Logger } from '../utils/Logger';

export interface FallbackPolicy {
  policyId: string;
  strategy: 'round-robin' | 'cost-optimized' | 'quota-aware' | 'latency-first';
  chain: ModelConfig[];
  onErrors: {
    quota_exhausted: 'fallback_next' | 'retry_then_fallback';
    rate_limited: 'retry_then_fallback' | 'fallback_next';
    provider_down: 'fallback_next';
  };
  budget?: {
    maxCostUsd: number;
    dailyLimit: number;
  };
}

export class ProviderFallbackService extends EventEmitter {
  private providers: ModelProvider[];
  private policies: Map<string, FallbackPolicy> = new Map();
  private quotaStatus: Map<string, QuotaStatus> = new Map();
  private failureCounts: Map<string, number> = new Map();
  private logger: Logger;
  private currentPolicyId: string = 'default';

  constructor(providers: ModelProvider[], defaultPolicy?: FallbackPolicy) {
    super();
    this.providers = providers;
    this.logger = new Logger('ProviderFallbackService');
    this.initializeQuotaTracking();
    if (defaultPolicy) {
      this.policies.set(defaultPolicy.policyId, defaultPolicy);
    }
  }

  private initializeQuotaTracking() {
    this.providers.forEach(p => {
      this.quotaStatus.set(p.id, {
        provider: p.id,
        rpm: { used: 0, limit: p.rpmLimit || Infinity, resetAt: new Date(Date.now() + 60000) },
        tpm: { used: 0, limit: p.tpmLimit || Infinity, resetAt: new Date(Date.now() + 60000) },
        dailyCost: { used: 0, limit: p.dailyBudget || Infinity, resetAt: new Date(Date.now() + 86400000) },
        isExhausted: false,
        lastError: null,
        consecutiveFailures: 0
      });
    });
  }

  public async selectProvider(taskType?: string): Promise<ModelConfig> {
    const policy = this.policies.get(this.currentPolicyId) || this.getDefaultPolicy();
    const availableChain = this.filterExhaustedProviders(policy.chain);

    if (availableChain.length === 0) {
      this.emit('all_providers_exhausted', { timestamp: new Date(), policy: policy.policyId });
      throw new Error('All providers in fallback chain exhausted');
    }

    const selected = availableChain[0];
    this.logger.info(`Selected provider: ${selected.model} (${selected.provider})`);
    return selected;
  }

  private filterExhaustedProviders(chain: ModelConfig[]): ModelConfig[] {
    return chain.filter(config => {
      const status = this.quotaStatus.get(config.provider);
      return status && !status.isExhausted;
    });
  }

  public reportError(providerId: string, error: Error) {
    const status = this.quotaStatus.get(providerId);
    if (!status) return;

    status.consecutiveFailures++;
    status.lastError = error.message;

    const errorType = this.classifyError(error);
    const policy = this.policies.get(this.currentPolicyId)!;
    const action = policy.onErrors[errorType];

    this.logger.warn(`Provider ${providerId} error: ${errorType} → Action: ${action}`);

    if (errorType === 'quota_exhausted' || status.consecutiveFailures >= 3) {
      status.isExhausted = true;
      this.emit('provider_exhausted', { providerId, errorType, timestamp: new Date() });
    }

    this.quotaStatus.set(providerId, status);
    this.emit('provider_error', { providerId, error: error.message, action });
  }

  private classifyError(error: Error): 'quota_exhausted' | 'rate_limited' | 'provider_down' {
    const message = error.message.toLowerCase();
    if (message.includes('quota') || message.includes('limit')) return 'quota_exhausted';
    if (message.includes('rate') || message.includes('429')) return 'rate_limited';
    return 'provider_down';
  }

  public registerPolicy(policy: FallbackPolicy) {
    this.policies.set(policy.policyId, policy);
    this.logger.info(`Registered fallback policy: ${policy.policyId}`);
  }

  public setActivePolicy(policyId: string) {
    if (this.policies.has(policyId)) {
      this.currentPolicyId = policyId;
      this.emit('policy_changed', { policyId });
    }
  }

  public getQuotaDashboard(): Map<string, QuotaStatus> {
    return new Map(this.quotaStatus);
  }

  public resetQuota(providerId: string) {
    const status = this.quotaStatus.get(providerId);
    if (status) {
      status.isExhausted = false;
      status.consecutiveFailures = 0;
      status.lastError = null;
      this.quotaStatus.set(providerId, status);
      this.emit('quota_reset', { providerId });
    }
  }

  private getDefaultPolicy(): FallbackPolicy {
    return {
      policyId: 'default',
      strategy: 'quota-aware',
      chain: this.providers.map(p => ({
        provider: p.id,
        model: p.defaultModel,
        priority: 1
      })),
      onErrors: {
        quota_exhausted: 'fallback_next',
        rate_limited: 'retry_then_fallback',
        provider_down: 'fallback_next'
      }
    };
  }
}
```

### 3.2 Session Guardian (`packages/core/src/services/SessionGuardian.ts`)

```typescript
// packages/core/src/services/SessionGuardian.ts
import { spawn, ChildProcess, SpawnOptions } from 'child_process';
import { EventEmitter } from 'events';
import { Logger } from '../utils/Logger';
import { SessionConfig, SessionState } from '../types/sessions';

export interface SessionHandle {
  sessionId: string;
  pid: number;
  status: 'running' | 'paused' | 'stopped' | 'crashed';
  startedAt: Date;
  lastHeartbeat: Date;
  worktree?: string;
  repo?: string;
}

export class SessionGuardian extends EventEmitter {
  private activeSessions: Map<string, SessionHandle> = new Map();
  private processMap: Map<string, ChildProcess> = new Map();
  private sessionConfigs: Map<string, SessionConfig> = new Map();
  private logger: Logger;
  private heartbeatInterval: number = 5000;
  private heartbeatTimer: NodeJS.Timeout | null = null;

  constructor() {
    super();
    this.logger = new Logger('SessionGuardian');
    this.startHeartbeatMonitor();
  }

  public startSession(sessionId: string, config: SessionConfig): SessionHandle {
    this.sessionConfigs.set(sessionId, config);
    const handle = this.spawnProcess(sessionId, config);
    this.activeSessions.set(sessionId, handle);
    this.emit('session_started', { sessionId, pid: handle.pid });
    return handle;
  }

  private spawnProcess(sessionId: string, config: SessionConfig): SessionHandle {
    const [cmd, ...args] = config.command.split(' ');
    
    const options: SpawnOptions = {
      env: { ...process.env, ...config.env, HYPERCODE_SESSION_ID: sessionId },
      cwd: config.cwd || process.cwd(),
      stdio: ['pipe', 'pipe', 'pipe'],
      detached: false
    };

    const child = spawn(cmd, args, options);
    this.processMap.set(sessionId, child);

    const handle: SessionHandle = {
      sessionId,
      pid: child.pid!,
      status: 'running',
      startedAt: new Date(),
      lastHeartbeat: new Date(),
      worktree: config.worktree,
      repo: config.repo
    };

    // Stream logs to WebUI
    child.stdout?.on('data', (data) => {
      this.emit('session_log', { sessionId, data: data.toString(), type: 'stdout' });
      handle.lastHeartbeat = new Date();
    });

    child.stderr?.on('data', (data) => {
      this.emit('session_log', { sessionId, data: data.toString(), type: 'stderr' });
      handle.lastHeartbeat = new Date();
    });

    // Handle crash/restart
    child.on('exit', (code, signal) => {
      handle.status = code === 0 ? 'stopped' : 'crashed';
      this.emit('session_exit', { sessionId, code, signal });
      
      if (config.autoRestart && code !== 0) {
        this.logger.warn(`Session ${sessionId} crashed (code ${code}). Restarting...`);
        this.emit('session_restarting', { sessionId, attempt: this.getRestartCount(sessionId) });
        setTimeout(() => this.restartSession(sessionId), config.restartDelay || 2000);
      }
    });

    child.on('error', (err) => {
      this.emit('session_error', { sessionId, error: err.message });
      handle.status = 'crashed';
    });

    return handle;
  }

  public stopSession(sessionId: string): void {
    const child = this.processMap.get(sessionId);
    const handle = this.activeSessions.get(sessionId);
    
    if (child) {
      child.kill('SIGTERM');
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (child.exitCode === null) child.kill('SIGKILL');
      }, 3000);
    }

    if (handle) {
      handle.status = 'stopped';
      this.activeSessions.set(sessionId, handle);
    }

    this.emit('session_stopped', { sessionId });
  }

  public restartSession(sessionId: string): SessionHandle {
    this.stopSession(sessionId);
    const config = this.sessionConfigs.get(sessionId);
    if (config) {
      return this.startSession(sessionId, config);
    }
    throw new Error(`Session config not found for ${sessionId}`);
  }

  public pauseSession(sessionId: string): void {
    const child = this.processMap.get(sessionId);
    if (child) {
      child.kill('SIGSTOP');
      const handle = this.activeSessions.get(sessionId);
      if (handle) {
        handle.status = 'paused';
        this.activeSessions.set(sessionId, handle);
      }
      this.emit('session_paused', { sessionId });
    }
  }

  public resumeSession(sessionId: string): void {
    const child = this.processMap.get(sessionId);
    if (child) {
      child.kill('SIGCONT');
      const handle = this.activeSessions.get(sessionId);
      if (handle) {
        handle.status = 'running';
        this.activeSessions.set(sessionId, handle);
      }
      this.emit('session_resumed', { sessionId });
    }
  }

  public getSessionState(sessionId: string): SessionHandle | undefined {
    return this.activeSessions.get(sessionId);
  }

  public getAllSessions(): SessionHandle[] {
    return Array.from(this.activeSessions.values());
  }

  private startHeartbeatMonitor() {
    this.heartbeatTimer = setInterval(() => {
      const now = new Date();
      for (const [sessionId, handle] of this.activeSessions.entries()) {
        const elapsed = now.getTime() - handle.lastHeartbeat.getTime();
        if (elapsed > 30000 && handle.status === 'running') {
          this.logger.warn(`Session ${sessionId} heartbeat timeout (${elapsed}ms)`);
          this.emit('session_heartbeat_timeout', { sessionId, elapsed });
        }
      }
    }, this.heartbeatInterval);
  }

  private getRestartCount(sessionId: string): number {
    // Track restart attempts for crash loop detection
    return 0; // Implement counter storage
  }

  public dispose() {
    if (this.heartbeatTimer) clearInterval(this.heartbeatTimer);
    for (const sessionId of this.activeSessions.keys()) {
      this.stopSession(sessionId);
    }
  }
}
```

### 3.3 WebUI Dashboard Component (`apps/web/src/components/dashboard/MissionControlDashboard.tsx`)

```tsx
// apps/web/src/components/dashboard/MissionControlDashboard.tsx
'use client';

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Card, CardHeader, CardTitle, CardContent } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Progress } from '@/components/ui/progress';
import { Activity, Terminal, Server, AlertCircle, RefreshCw, Play, Pause, StopCircle } from 'lucide-react';
import { trpc } from '@/utils/trpc';

interface SystemStats {
  cpu: number;
  ram: number;
  disk: number;
  network: number;
  activeSessions: number;
}

interface Session {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  model: string;
  status: 'running' | 'paused' | 'stopped' | 'crashed';
  uptime: string;
  lastActivity: string;
}

interface ProviderQuota {
  provider: string;
  model: string;
  rpmUsed: number;
  rpmLimit: number;
  tpmUsed: number;
  tpmLimit: number;
  dailyCost: number;
  dailyBudget: number;
  isExhausted: boolean;
}

export function MissionControlDashboard() {
  const [stats, setStats] = useState<SystemStats>({ cpu: 0, ram: 0, disk: 0, network: 0, activeSessions: 0 });
  const [sessions, setSessions] = useState<Session[]>([]);
  const [quotas, setQuotas] = useState<ProviderQuota[]>([]);

  // Real-time WebSocket connection
  useEffect(() => {
    const ws = new WebSocket('ws://localhost:3001/ws/mission-control');
    
    ws.onmessage = (event) => {
      const data = JSON.parse(event.data);
      switch (data.type) {
        case 'stats':
          setStats(data.payload);
          break;
        case 'sessions':
          setSessions(data.payload);
          break;
        case 'quotas':
          setQuotas(data.payload);
          break;
      }
    };

    return () => ws.close();
  }, []);

  // tRPC mutations for session control
  const restartSession = trpc.sessions.restart.useMutation();
  const pauseSession = trpc.sessions.pause.useMutation();
  const stopSession = trpc.sessions.stop.useMutation();

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-4 p-4 bg-slate-950 min-h-screen">
      {/* Row 1: System Health */}
      <Card className="bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 text-white">
        <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
          <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">CPU Usage</CardTitle>
          <Activity className="h-4 w-4 text-green-400" />
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{stats.cpu}%</div>
          <Progress value={stats.cpu} className="mt-2" />
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      <Card className="bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 text-white">
        <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
          <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">RAM Usage</CardTitle>
          <Server className="h-4 w-4 text-blue-400" />
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{stats.ram}%</div>
          <Progress value={stats.ram} className="mt-2" />
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      <Card className="bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 text-white">
        <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
          <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">Active Sessions</CardTitle>
          <Terminal className="h-4 w-4 text-purple-400" />
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{stats.activeSessions}</div>
          <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">Supervised by Guardian</p>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      <Card className="bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 text-white">
        <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
          <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">System Health</CardTitle>
          <Activity className="h-4 w-4 text-emerald-400" />
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold">🟢 Operational</div>
          <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">All services running</p>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      {/* Row 2: Active Sessions */}
      <Card className="col-span-1 md:col-span-2 lg:col-span-2 bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 text-white">
        <CardHeader>
          <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <Terminal className="h-5 w-5" />
            Session Orchestrator
          </CardTitle>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="space-y-2">
            {sessions.map(session => (
              <div key={session.id} className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-slate-800 rounded-lg">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  <Badge variant={session.status === 'running' ? 'default' : session.status === 'crashed' ? 'destructive' : 'secondary'}>
                    {session.status}
                  </Badge>
                  <div>
                    <span className="font-mono text-sm font-medium">{session.name}</span>
                    <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">{session.model} • {session.uptime}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="flex gap-2">
                  <Button size="sm" variant="outline" onClick={() => pauseSession.mutate({ sessionId: session.id })}>
                    <Pause className="h-3 w-3" />
                  </Button>
                  <Button size="sm" variant="outline" onClick={() => restartSession.mutate({ sessionId: session.id })}>
                    <RefreshCw className="h-3 w-3" />
                  </Button>
                  <Button size="sm" variant="outline" onClick={() => stopSession.mutate({ sessionId: session.id })}>
                    <StopCircle className="h-3 w-3" />
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
            {sessions.length === 0 && (
              <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm text-center py-4">No active sessions</p>
            )}
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      {/* Row 2: Provider Quotas */}
      <Card className="col-span-1 md:col-span-2 lg:col-span-2 bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 text-white">
        <CardHeader>
          <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <Server className="h-5 w-5" />
            Provider Quotas
          </CardTitle>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {quotas.map(quota => (
              <div key={quota.provider} className="p-3 bg-slate-800 rounded-lg">
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
                  <span className="font-medium">{quota.provider}</span>
                  {quota.isExhausted ? (
                    <Badge variant="destructive">Exhausted</Badge>
                  ) : (
                    <Badge variant="default">Active</Badge>
                  )}
                </div>
                <div className="space-y-1">
                  <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                    <span>RPM: {quota.rpmUsed}/{quota.rpmLimit}</span>
                    <span>${quota.dailyCost}/${quota.dailyBudget}</span>
                  </div>
                  <Progress value={(quota.rpmUsed / quota.rpmLimit) * 100} className="h-2" />
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
}
```

**Assistant - --**

Yes — and the responses you collected are broadly converging on the same correct direction.

# Bottom line

You should proceed with a **TypeScript-first, WebUI-first, plugin-capable architecture** with:

- **main control plane in Node/TypeScript**
- **worker threads for internal planning/orchestration**
- **child processes for crash-prone / external runtimes**
- **Python sidecars only where already justified**
- **Go/Rust only later for proven bottlenecks**
- **MCP treated as an interface layer, not the sole implementation path**
- **automatic provider/model fallback as the immediate P0**
- **dashboard-first exposure of every important capability**

Given your repo, your current maturity level, and your actual feature goals, this is the right path.

---

# What the model outputs got right

Across those responses, the strongest common recommendations were:

- keep the core in **TypeScript**
- prioritize **provider fallback**
- build a **session supervisor**
- make the **WebUI the main control surface**
- isolate workloads via **worker threads + child processes**
- normalize external tools behind **adapters/plugins**
- create a **research/index pipeline** instead of doing ad hoc ingestion
- stop over-investing in narrow swarm analytics before the core operator experience is excellent

I agree with all of that.

---

# My recommendation: the actual next move

Do **not** try to attack “all feature parity for all referenced tools” as one undifferentiated stream.

Instead, define the next implementation arc as:

## Phase 122–126: Operator Reality Closure

- **ExecutionSupervisor**

That is the pragmatic path.

# Direct answer to your architecture question

## Should Hypercode use Go or Java?

### Use TypeScript as the primary architecture.
Because you need:

- shared backend/frontend types
- fastest feature iteration
- direct integration with current code
- best compatibility with MCP ecosystem
- dashboard/browser/extension coherence
- simpler plugin model

### Use Go later only if needed for narrow infrastructure services:
- PTY/session multiplexer
- high-throughput proxy/transport daemon
- telemetry collector
- process watchdog daemon

### Do not use Java for the main system.
It adds operational and architectural complexity without helping your core product goals.

---

# The most important architectural correction

Your system should not think in terms of:

- “MCP or not MCP?”

It should think in terms of:

## “Every capability has one internal contract, and multiple possible execution modes.”

For any subsystem, support these modes:

- **Native**
- **Wrapped**
- **Process**
- **MCP-exposed**
- **UI-managed**

That gives you the flexibility you want:
- built in by default
- still usable via MCP
- still wrappable from reference tools
- still manageable from dashboard

---

# The core architectural shape I recommend

## 1. Control plane
Long-running Hypercode kernel.

Responsibilities:
- provider registry
- model routing
- session registry
- plugin registry
- tool registry
- auth/secrets
- event bus
- dashboard API
- policy engine

## 2. Execution plane
Where work actually runs.

Use:
- **worker threads** for internal trusted orchestration
- **child processes** for external CLIs, MCP servers, browser tasks, sandboxes
- **sidecars** for Python-heavy jobs

## 3. Integration plane
Adapters that normalize:
- providers
- harnesses
- MCP servers
- memory backends
- browser integrations
- git/worktree systems
- research ingestion sources

## 4. Experience plane
Primary operator surfaces:
- WebUI
- CLI
- browser extension

The **WebUI should be the primary console**.

---

# The single highest-priority feature

You explicitly called this out, and you are correct:

## Automatic model/provider fallback is the most important immediate feature.

Because without it:
- sessions stall
- autopilot stalls
- councils stall
- swarm stalls
- long-running automation becomes brittle
- subscription/API hybrid usage remains clumsy

So this must be treated as a **platform subsystem**, not an agent-side hack.

---

# What to build immediately

## 1. `ProviderRouter`
Responsible for:
- provider/model selection
- fallback chains
- capability matching
- free-tier/subscription/API preference
- quota-aware routing
- auth-aware routing
- task-based selection

## 2. `FallbackPolicyEngine`
Responsible for:
- ordered fallback rules
- quota exhaustion handling
- rate-limit handling
- provider-down handling
- budget caps
- quality floors
- cooldown windows
- rationale logging

## 3. `QuotaTracker`
Track:
- request rate
- token rate
- daily/monthly spend
- reset windows
- auth/subscription status
- recent failures

## 4. Provider dashboard
Must include:
- provider auth state
- quota bars
- fallback chain editor
- per-session auto/manual routing mode
- “why this model was selected”
- live failover events

This is one of the most valuable UI panels in the whole product.

---

# The second highest-priority feature

## Session supervision

You want to run and supervise:
- Hypercode-native sessions
- opencode-like sessions
- superai-cli-like sessions
- cloud sessions
- future external harness sessions

That means you need a proper:

## `SessionRuntimeManager` + `ExecutionSupervisor`

### `SessionRuntimeManager`
Tracks:
- session ID
- runtime kind
- repo binding
- worktree binding
- provider policy
- status
- heartbeat
- last action
- history snapshot
- restart metadata

### `ExecutionSupervisor`
Handles:
- spawn
- stop
- restart
- crash detection
- exponential backoff
- crash loop detection
- log capture
- CPU/memory telemetry
- auto-resume policy

This is your “AI OS process manager.”

# What to do about the 900+ submodules / references

Your vision is powerful, but you need discipline or the repo becomes unmanageable.

## Add an explicit integration tier model

### Tier A — Core parity targets
- native implementation planned
- deep documentation
- adapter/wrapper if needed
- dashboard surfaced

### Tier B — Plugin/reference candidates
- indexed
- summarized
- optional adapter
- not yet parity target

### Tier C — Directory/reference only
- metadata + summary only
- maybe submodule, maybe link-only
- no immediate integration

### Tier D — Rejected / irrelevant / stale
- tracked explicitly
- excluded from active roadmap

This lets the research pipeline remain broad without making execution chaotic.

---

# The “research every link” requirement

This should become a formal subsystem, not a loose aspiration.

## Build a `KnowledgeIngestionManager`

Pipeline:

1. **Discover**
   - URLs from docs, submodules, issues, readmes, linked pages

2. **Normalize**
   - dedupe repo/docs/issues/forks/upstreams

3. **Classify**
   - repo, docs, article, issue, benchmark, concept, noise

4. **Enrich**
   - metadata, summary, features, architecture, relevance

5. **Decide**
   - submodule / mirror-docs / index-only / reject / defer

6. **Emit**
   - structured record
   - docs summary
   - category placement
   - integration note
   - parity-gap note

7. **Review continuously**
   - upstream changes
   - stale entries
   - parity tracking

That’s how your vision becomes maintainable.

---

# Important correction on concurrency

You asked about “each model on a different thread.”

That is close, but the better design is:

## Each runtime unit gets the right isolation boundary.

### Worker threads
Use for:
- planning
- summarization
- reranking
- context compaction
- light agent logic
- policy evaluation

### Child processes
Use for:
- long-running coding sessions
- external CLIs
- MCP servers
- browser/computer-use runtimes
- untrusted tools
- sandboxes

### Sidecars
Use for:
- OCR
- heavy RAG/document work
- Python-native pipelines

So the abstraction should be:
- **one runtime = one managed execution container appropriate to workload and risk**
not
- **one model = one raw JS thread**

---

# The best package structure from here

I recommend evolving toward this:

```text
apps/
  web/
  extension/
  cli/

packages/
  core/
  runtime/
  providers/
  sessions/
  agents/
  tools/
  mcp/
  memory/
  rag/
  research/
  auth/
  telemetry/
  git/
  browser/
  plugins/
  schemas/
  ui-contracts/
  harnesses/

services/
  python-rag/
  browser-automation/
  system-proxy/
```

This is much closer to your actual product shape.

---

# What to stop doing

For now, stop spending major effort on ultra-granular swarm analytics unless they support an operator-facing core workflow.

You have already built a lot of sophistication there. Good. But the product now needs:

- provider resilience
- session resilience
- dashboard clarity
- tool management clarity
- memory usability
- harness supervision

That is what will make Hypercode feel real as a daily operator console.

### 3.1 Provider Fallback Chain Editor (LIVE)
```tsx
// apps/web/src/components/providers/FallbackChainEditor.tsx
import { api } from '@/utils/trpc';
import { DragDropContext, Droppable, Draggable } from '@hello-pangea/dnd';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';

export const FallbackChainEditor = () => {
  const { data: chain } = api.providers.getFallbackChain.useQuery();
  const mutateChain = api.providers.updateFallbackChain.useMutation();

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <h3>Quota-Aware Fallback Chain</h3>
      <DragDropContext onDragEnd={handleReorder}>
        <Droppable droppableId="chain">
          {(provided) => (
            <ul {...provided.droppableProps} ref={provided.innerRef}>
              {chain?.map((model, idx) => (
                <Draggable key={model.id} draggableId={model.id} index={idx}>
                  {(provided) => (
                    <li ref={provided.innerRef} {...provided.draggableProps} {...provided.dragHandleProps}>
                      <Badge>{model.provider}:{model.name} ({model.quota.remaining}%)</Badge>
                    </li>
                  )}
                </Draggable>
              ))}
              {provided.placeholder}
            </ul>
          )}
        </Droppable>
      </DragDropContext>
      <details>
        <summary>Policy Docs</summary>
        <ul>
          <li>Quota Exhaust → Next (e.g., Claude → Gemini)</li>
          <li>Rate-Limit → Retry (3x) → Fallback</li>
          <li>Free-Tier Opt: OpenRouter/Copilot First</li>
        </ul>
      </details>
      <Button onClick={() => mutateChain.mutate({ chain })}>Save & Test</Button>
    </div>
  );
};
```

### 3.2 Session Supervision Grid (LIVE: Autostart/Restart Opencode/etc.)
```tsx
// apps/web/src/components/sessions/SupervisionGrid.tsx
import { api } from '@/utils/trpc';
import { Card, Badge, Button } from '@/components/ui';

export const SupervisionGrid = () => {
  const sessions = api.sessions.list.useQuery();
  const restart = api.sessions.restart.useMutation();

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
      {sessions.data?.map((s) => (
        <Card key={s.id}>
          <CardHeader>
            <h4>{s.dir} ({s.harness})</h4>
            <Badge variant={s.status === 'running' ? 'default' : 'destructive'}>{s.status}</Badge>
          </CardHeader>
          <CardContent className="space-y-2">
            <p>Model: {s.model} | Crashes: {s.restartCount}</p>
            <div className="flex gap-2">
              <Button size="sm" onClick={() => restart.mutate({ id: s.id })}>Restart</Button>
              <Button size="sm" variant="outline">Broadcast</Button>
              <Button size="sm" variant="ghost">Council Review</Button>
            </div>
            <details>
              <summary>Auto-Policy</summary>
              <ul>
                <li>Restart: Always (3s delay)</li>
                <li>Supervisor: Council (Arch/Guard/Opt)</li>
                <li>Fallback Prompts: Cycle 5</li>
              </ul>
            </details>
          </CardContent>
        </Card>
      ))}
      <Card>
        <Button className="w-full h-full">+ New Session (Opencode/etc.)</Button>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
};
```

**New Operator Panels**:
- **Mission Control**: Health strips + Quick Actions.
- **Providers**: OAuth buttons (Claude Max → Live) + Quota Bars/Resets.
- **Sessions**: Grid w/ Autopilot toggles (harnesses: Opencode/Codebuff/Codex/etc.).
- **Inline Docs**: Every elem → `<details>` (features/policy).

The total session cost is aggregated across all n tool calls and agent loops:

Queue: You paste a URL or trigger a scan of .gitmodules.
Scrape: A lightweight model (e.g., gemini-1.5-flash or gpt-4o-mini) clones/fetches the README.md and repo tree.
Synthesize: The model extracts capabilities and maps them to our Reference Categories.
Index: Results are saved to HYPERCODE_MASTER_INDEX.jsonc and embedded into the local ChromaDB.

🔴 Phase 122: Provider Fallback Engine (CRITICAL — Week 1)
Every model agreed this is the single highest-impact feature. Without it, autonomous operation is impossible.


// packages/ai/src/fallback/engine.ts
// Consolidated design from all 7 model recommendations

interface FallbackPolicy {
  id: string;
  name: string;                    // e.g., "default-coding"
  strategy: 
    | 'ordered'                    // strict priority order
    | 'quota-aware'                // skip exhausted, prefer freshest
    | 'cost-optimized'             // cheapest available first
    | 'latency-first'             // fastest response time
    | 'capability-match'           // best fit for task type
    | 'cost_per_success_then_latency'; // GPT-5.3's hybrid suggestion
  
  chain: ProviderModelPair[];      // ordered fallback list
  
  onErrors: {
    quota_exhausted: 'fallback_next' | 'wait_and_retry';
    rate_limited: 'retry_then_fallback' | 'fallback_next';
    auth_failure: 'skip_provider' | 'refresh_and_retry';
    provider_down: 'fallback_next';
    timeout: 'retry_same' | 'fallback_next';
  };
  
  budget?: {
    maxDailyCostUsd: number;
    maxMonthlyCostUsd: number;
  };
  
  preferences?: {
    preferFreeFirst: boolean;       // Use free tiers before paid
    preferSubscriptionBeforeAPI: boolean;  // OAuth > API key
    stayInModelFamily: boolean;     // Try all providers of same model first
  };
}

interface QuotaState {
  providerId: string;
  rpm: { used: number; limit: number; resetAt: Date };
  tpm: { used: number; limit: number; resetAt: Date };
  dailyCost: { used: number; budget: number };
  isExhausted: boolean;
  lastError?: { code: string; at: Date };
  cooldownUntil?: Date;
}

// The core router — all models agreed on this pattern
class FallbackOrchestrator {
  private quotaStore: Map<string, QuotaState>;
  private policies: Map<string, FallbackPolicy>;
  
  async execute(
    task: AgenticTask, 
    policyId: string = 'default'
  ): Promise<ModelResponse> {
    const policy = this.policies.get(policyId)!;
    const chain = this.resolveChain(policy, task);
    
    for (const provider of chain) {
      const quota = this.quotaStore.get(provider.id);
      
      // Skip exhausted/cooling providers
      if (quota?.isExhausted || quota?.cooldownUntil > Date.now()) {
        this.emitTelemetry('skipped', provider, 'exhausted');
        continue;
      }
      
      try {
        const result = await this.callProvider(provider, task);
        this.trackUsage(provider, result);
        this.emitTelemetry('success', provider, result);
        return result;
      } catch (e) {
        const action = this.classifyError(e, policy);
        this.emitTelemetry('error', provider, { error: e, action });
        
        if (action === 'retry_then_fallback') {
          // Exponential backoff retry (max 2 attempts)
          const retry = await this.retryWithBackoff(provider, task, 2);
          if (retry) return retry;
        }
        
        if (action === 'fallback_next') continue;
        if (action === 'refresh_and_retry') {
          await this.refreshAuth(provider);
          continue; // Will retry this provider on next loop
        }
      }
    }
    
    throw new AllProvidersExhaustedError(chain, this.quotaStore);
  }
  
  // Kimi's suggestion: persist decision telemetry
  private emitTelemetry(
    type: string, 
    provider: ProviderModelPair, 
    data: any
  ) {
    this.eventBus.emit('provider:decision', {
      type,
      provider: provider.id,
      model: provider.model,
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      ...data
    });
  }
}

Google	OAuth (AI Plus) + API	Gemini Flash free	AI Plus $20/mo	✅

xAI (Grok)	API	—	—	✅

// packages/core/src/agentic-loop/loop.ts
// The actual coding engine — what makes Hypercode a coding tool

interface AgenticLoop {
  execute(task: string, context: SessionContext): AsyncIterableIterator<LoopEvent>;
}

type LoopEvent = 
  | { type: 'thinking'; content: string }
  | { type: 'tool_call'; tool: string; params: Record<string, any> }
  | { type: 'tool_result'; tool: string; result: any; durationMs: number }
  | { type: 'edit'; file: string; diff: string }
  | { type: 'message'; content: string }
  | { type: 'context_compact'; removed: number; harvested: number }
  | { type: 'model_switch'; from: string; to: string; reason: string }
  | { type: 'complete'; summary: string }
  | { type: 'error'; error: Error; recovery?: string };

// Core tools available to the agentic loop
const CORE_TOOLS = {
  // File operations
  read_file: { /* read with line numbers, range support */ },
  write_file: { /* create or overwrite */ },
  edit_file: { /* surgical edits with search/replace blocks */ },
  list_directory: { /* recursive with gitignore respect */ },
  
  // Execution
  bash: { /* with timeout, cwd, env control */ },
  
  // Search
  grep: { /* ripgrep-powered */ },
  semantic_search: { /* embedding-based code search */ },
  find_definition: { /* LSP go-to-definition */ },
  find_references: { /* LSP find-references */ },
  
  // Git
  git_status: {},
  git_diff: {},
  git_commit: {},
  git_log: {},
  
  // Web
  web_search: {},
  fetch_url: {},
  
  // Context
  compact_context: { /* harvest + prune + summarize */ },
  store_memory: { /* save to long-term memory */ },
  recall_memory: { /* semantic memory search */ },
};

// Context manager — automatic compaction when approaching limit
class ContextManager {
  private messages: Message[] = [];
  private tokenCount: number = 0;
  private readonly tokenLimit: number;
  private readonly compactionThreshold: number; // e.g., 0.85
  
  async addMessage(msg: Message): Promise<void> {
    this.messages.push(msg);
    this.tokenCount += estimateTokens(msg);
    
    if (this.tokenCount / this.tokenLimit > this.compactionThreshold) {
      await this.autoCompact();
    }
  }
  
  private async autoCompact(): Promise<void> {
    // 1. Harvest key information into memory
    const harvested = await this.harvester.extract(this.messages);
    await this.memoryStore.storeAll(harvested);
    
    // 2. Summarize older messages
    const summary = await this.summarizer.summarize(
      this.messages.slice(0, -10) // Keep last 10 messages intact
    );
    
    // 3. Replace with summary + recent
    this.messages = [
      { role: 'system', content: summary },
      ...this.messages.slice(-10)
    ];
    
    this.tokenCount = this.messages.reduce(
      (sum, m) => sum + estimateTokens(m), 0
    );
  }
}

// SystemHealthStrip — real-time hardware monitoring
function SystemHealthStrip() {
  const { data } = api.system.health.useQuery(undefined, { 
    refetchInterval: 2000 
  });
  
  return (
    <div className="flex gap-4 p-3 bg-slate-900/50 rounded-lg border border-slate-700">
      <MetricPill label="CPU" value={data?.cpu} unit="%" 
        color={data?.cpu > 80 ? 'red' : data?.cpu > 50 ? 'yellow' : 'green'} />
      <MetricPill label="RAM" value={data?.ram} unit="%" 
        color={data?.ram > 85 ? 'red' : 'green'} />
      <MetricPill label="GPU" value={data?.gpu} unit="%" />
      <MetricPill label="Disk" value={data?.disk} unit="%" />
      <MetricPill label="MCP" value={data?.mcpServers} unit=" active" />
      <MetricPill label="Sessions" value={data?.activeSessions} unit=" running" />
      <MetricPill label="Memory" value={data?.memoryCount} unit=" entries" />
    </div>
  );
}

// ProviderQuotaCard — the fallback chain visualizer
function ProviderQuotaCard() {
  const { data: providers } = api.providers.quotaStatus.useQuery();
  const { data: chain } = api.providers.fallbackChain.useQuery();
  
  return (
    <Card className="bg-slate-900 border-slate-700">
      <CardHeader>
        <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Zap className="h-5 w-5 text-yellow-400" />
          Provider Quotas
        </CardTitle>
        {chain && (
          <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">
            Fallback: {chain.map(c => c.name).join(' → ')}
            <Button variant="ghost" size="xs" className="ml-2">Edit</Button>
          </p>
        )}
      </CardHeader>
      <CardContent className="space-y-3">
        {providers?.map(p => (
          <ProviderQuotaBar key={p.id} provider={p} />
        ))}
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}

function ProviderQuotaBar({ provider }: { provider: ProviderQuota }) {
  const pctUsed = (provider.rpm.used / provider.rpm.limit) * 100;
  const color = pctUsed > 90 ? 'bg-red-500' : pctUsed > 70 ? 'bg-yellow-500' : 'bg-green-500';
  
  return (
    <div className="space-y-1">
      <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
        <span className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <ProviderIcon id={provider.id} />
          {provider.name}
          {provider.authMethod === 'oauth' && (
            <Badge variant="outline" className="text-[10px]">
              {provider.oauthConnected ? '✅ Connected' : '⚠️ Not connected'}
            </Badge>
          )}
        </span>
        <span className="text-slate-400">
          {provider.rpm.used}/{provider.rpm.limit} RPM
          {provider.resetIn && ` · Resets ${provider.resetIn}`}
        </span>
      </div>
      <div className="h-2 bg-slate-700 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
        <div className={`h-full ${color} rounded-full transition-all`} 
             style={{ width: `${pctUsed}%` }} />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
🔴 Phase 125: Session Supervisor & Auto-Restart (Week 2)

// packages/core/src/sessions/supervisor.ts
// Consolidated from Qwen's SessionGuardian + GPT-5.4's ExecutionSupervisor

import { ChildProcess, spawn } from 'child_process';
import { EventEmitter } from 'events';

interface SessionRuntime {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  harness: 'hypercode-native' | 'opencode' | 'claude-code' | 'codex' | 
           'gemini-cli' | 'superai-cli' | 'codebuff' | string;
  status: 'starting' | 'running' | 'paused' | 'crashed' | 'stopped';
  
  // Bindings
  cwd: string;
  worktree?: string;
  providerId?: string;
  modelPolicyId?: string;
  
  // Supervision
  autoRestart: boolean;
  maxRestarts: number;
  restartCount: number;
  restartBackoffMs: number;
  crashLoopDetected: boolean;
  
  // Telemetry
  pid?: number;
  startedAt?: Date;
  lastActivityAt?: Date;
  tokensUsed?: number;
  costUsd?: number;
  
  // Process handle (not serialized)
  process?: ChildProcess;
}

class SessionSupervisor extends EventEmitter {
  private sessions = new Map<string, SessionRuntime>();
  private heartbeatInterval: NodeJS.Timer;
  
  constructor(private db: Database, private eventBus: EventBus) {
    super();
    // Restore sessions from DB on startup
    this.restoreSessions();
    // Heartbeat check every 10s
    this.heartbeatInterval = setInterval(() => this.checkHealth(), 10000);
  }
  
  async startSession(config: StartSessionConfig): Promise<SessionRuntime> {
    const session: SessionRuntime = {
      id: crypto.randomUUID(),
      name: config.name,
      harness: config.harness,
      status: 'starting',
      cwd: config.cwd,
      autoRestart: config.autoRestart ?? true,
      maxRestarts: config.maxRestarts ?? 10,
      restartCount: 0,
      restartBackoffMs: 1000,
      crashLoopDetected: false,
    };
    
    this.sessions.set(session.id, session);
    await this.spawnProcess(session);
    await this.db.sessions.upsert(session);
    
    return session;
  }
  
  private async spawnProcess(session: SessionRuntime): Promise<void> {
    const cmd = this.getCommand(session.harness, session);
    const proc = spawn(cmd.bin, cmd.args, {
      cwd: session.cwd,
      env: { ...process.env, ...cmd.env },
      stdio: ['pipe', 'pipe', 'pipe'],
    });
    
    session.process = proc;
    session.pid = proc.pid;
    session.status = 'running';
    session.startedAt = new Date();
    
    proc.stdout?.on('data', (data: Buffer) => {
      session.lastActivityAt = new Date();
      this.eventBus.emit('session:output', { 
        sessionId: session.id, 
        data: data.toString(), 
        stream: 'stdout' 
      });
    });
    
    proc.stderr?.on('data', (data: Buffer) => {
      this.eventBus.emit('session:output', { 
        sessionId: session.id, 
        data: data.toString(), 
        stream: 'stderr' 
      });
    });
    
    proc.on('exit', (code, signal) => {
      session.status = 'crashed';
      session.process = undefined;
      
      this.eventBus.emit('session:exit', { 
        sessionId: session.id, code, signal 
      });
      
      if (session.autoRestart && !session.crashLoopDetected) {
        this.scheduleRestart(session);
      }
    });
    
    this.eventBus.emit('session:started', { 
      sessionId: session.id, 
      pid: proc.pid 
    });
  }
  
  private scheduleRestart(session: SessionRuntime): void {
    session.restartCount++;
    
    if (session.restartCount >= session.maxRestarts) {
      session.crashLoopDetected = true;
      session.status = 'stopped';
      this.eventBus.emit('session:crash_loop', { sessionId: session.id });
      return;
    }
    
    const delay = Math.min(
      session.restartBackoffMs * Math.pow(2, session.restartCount - 1),
      30000 // Max 30s backoff
    );
    
    this.eventBus.emit('session:restarting', { 
      sessionId: session.id, 
      delayMs: delay,
      attempt: session.restartCount 
    });
    
    setTimeout(() => this.spawnProcess(session), delay);
  }
  
  private getCommand(
    harness: string, 
    session: SessionRuntime
  ): { bin: string; args: string[]; env: Record<string, string> } {
    switch (harness) {
      case 'hypercode-native':
        return { bin: 'node', args: ['packages/cli/dist/index.js', '--dir', session.cwd], env: {} };
      case 'opencode':
        return { bin: 'opencode', args: ['--dir', session.cwd], env: {} };
      case 'claude-code':
        return { bin: 'claude', args: ['--dir', session.cwd], env: {} };
      case 'codex':
        return { bin: 'codex', args: [session.cwd], env: {} };
      case 'gemini-cli':
        return { bin: 'gemini', args: ['--dir', session.cwd], env: {} };
      default:
        return { bin: harness, args: ['--dir', session.cwd], env: {} };
    }
  }
  
  // WebSocket streaming to dashboard
  getSessionStream(sessionId: string): ReadableStream<SessionEvent> {
    // Returns a stream that the dashboard can consume via WebSocket
    // for real-time log viewing
  }
  
  async broadcastToAll(message: string): Promise<void> {
    for (const [id, session] of this.sessions) {
      if (session.status === 'running' && session.process?.stdin) {
        session.process.stdin.write(message + '\n');
      }
    }
  }
}

function SessionCard({ session }: { session: SessionRuntime }) {
  const [showTerminal, setShowTerminal] = useState(false);
  
  return (
    <Card className="bg-slate-900 border-slate-700">
      <CardHeader className="pb-2">
        <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
          <div>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <StatusDot status={session.status} />
              <span className="font-mono text-sm">{session.cwd}</span>
            </div>
            <p className="text-xs text-slate-400 mt-1">
              {session.harness} · {session.providerId || 'auto'} · 
              {session.tokensUsed?.toLocaleString() || 0} tokens ·
              ${session.costUsd?.toFixed(2) || '0.00'}
            </p>
          </div>
          <div className="flex gap-1">
            <Button size="icon" variant="ghost" 
              onClick={() => setShowTerminal(!showTerminal)}>
              <Terminal className="h-4 w-4" />
            </Button>
            <Button size="icon" variant="ghost"
              onClick={() => restartSession.mutate(session.id)}>
              <RotateCw className="h-4 w-4" />
            </Button>
            <Button size="icon" variant="ghost"
              onClick={() => stopSession.mutate(session.id)}>
              <Square className="h-4 w-4" />
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </CardHeader>
      {showTerminal && (
        <CardContent className="pt-0">
          <div className="h-48 bg-black rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
            <WebTerminal sessionId={session.id} />
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      )}
    </Card>
  );
}

🟡 Phase 127-131: MCP Router Polish (Week 3-4)

// packages/mcp/src/toon-formatter.ts
// TOON Format — Tool-Optimized Output Notation

export function formatToolAsTOON(tool: MCPTool): string {
  // Convert verbose JSON schema to minimal context representation
  // Example: "read_file(path:str, range?:str) → str — Read file content"
  const params = tool.inputSchema.properties 
    ? Object.entries(tool.inputSchema.properties)
        .map(([name, schema]: [string, any]) => {
          const required = tool.inputSchema.required?.includes(name);
          const type = schema.type || 'any';
          return `${name}${required ? '' : '?'}:${type}`;
        })
        .join(', ')
    : '';
  
  return `${tool.name}(${params}) → ${tool.outputType || 'any'} — ${tool.description}`;
}

// Code Mode — represent tools as callable functions
export function formatToolAsCode(tool: MCPTool): string {
  return `async function ${tool.name}(${formatParams(tool)}): Promise<${tool.outputType || 'any'}> { /* ${tool.description} */ }`;
}

// Progressive Tool Disclosure
export class ProgressiveToolLoader {
  private allTools: MCPTool[];
  private disclosedTools: Set<string> = new Set();
  private embeddings: Map<string, number[]> = new Map();
  
  getRelevantTools(taskDescription: string, maxTools: number = 20): MCPTool[] {
    // 1. Always include essential tools (file, bash, search)
    const essential = this.allTools.filter(t => t.essential);
    
    // 2. Semantic search for task-relevant tools
    const taskEmbedding = this.embed(taskDescription);
    const ranked = this.allTools
      .filter(t => !t.essential)
      .map(t => ({
        tool: t,
        score: cosineSimilarity(taskEmbedding, this.embeddings.get(t.name)!)
      }))
      .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score)
      .slice(0, maxTools - essential.length);
    
    return [...essential, ...ranked.map(r => r.tool)];
  }
}

Isolation Rules (unanimous):

Agent/model crash → kills only that worker thread, auto-restart
MCP server crash → child process restarts, circuit breaker after 3 failures
CLI session crash → auto-restart with exponential backoff, max 10 retries
Main process → never crashes from child/worker failures (supervisor pattern)

Reasoning
Based on the comprehensive analysis across all model providers, here is the definitive Phase 122 implementation blueprint to achieve UI/functionality parity and the critical Provider Fallback system.

1. Architecture Decision: The Cellular TypeScript OS
Decision: Pure TypeScript/Node.js with Strategic Process Isolation

We remain TypeScript-native for ecosystem compatibility (MCP SDK, Vercel AI SDK, shared types with React dashboard), but implement a "Cellular Architecture" for fault tolerance:


┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    CONTROL PLANE (Main Process)                 │
│  packages/core                                                  │
│  • Express/tRPC/WebSocket API                                   │
│  • ProviderRouter & FallbackPolicyEngine                        │
│  • SessionRuntimeRegistry                                       │
│  • Configuration/Auth                                           │
└──────────────┬──────────────────────────────┬───────────────────┘
               │                              │
    ┌──────────▼──────────┐      ┌───────────▼────────────┐
    │   AGENT WORKERS     │      │   SESSION RUNTIMES     │
    │   (Worker Threads)  │      │   (Child Processes)    │
    │  • Prompt planning  │      │  • External CLIs       │
    │  • Context ranking  │      │  • MCP Servers         │
    │  • Tool selection   │      │  • Browser automation  │
    │  • Crash isolation  │      │  • Code sandboxes      │
    └──────────┬──────────┘      └───────────┬────────────┘
               │                              │
    ┌──────────▼──────────────────────────────▼────────────┐
    │              REDIS MESH BUS (Pub/Sub)                │
    │   • Cross-cell state sync                            │
    │   • Swarm coordination                               │
    │   • Artifact federation                              │
    └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
Crash Boundaries:

Level 1: Try/catch around tool calls (expected)
Level 2: Worker termination + respawn (model crash)
Level 3: Process restart + session recovery (CLI/MCP crash)
Level 4: Circuit breakers (provider quota exhaustion)
2. Phase 122: Critical Implementation Path
P0: Provider Fallback Engine (Unblocks Everything)
New Service: packages/core/src/providers/FallbackPolicyEngine.ts


interface FallbackChain {
  chainId: string;
  strategy: 'cost-optimized' | 'latency-first' | 'quota-aware' | 'quality-preserve';
  providers: ProviderConfig[];
  quotaTracking: Map<string, QuotaStatus>;
  onExhaustion: 'pause' | 'local-fallback' | 'notify-user';
}

export class FallbackPolicyEngine extends EventEmitter {
  // Real-time quota monitoring
  async executeWithFallback(task: Task, chain: FallbackChain): AsyncIterable<StreamChunk> {
    for (const provider of chain.providers) {
      try {
        return await this.execute(task, provider);
      } catch (e) {
        if (e.code === 'QUOTA_EXHAUSTED' || e.code === 'RATE_LIMIT') {
          this.emit('provider_exhausted', { provider, task });
          await this.quotaTracker.markExhausted(provider.id);
          continue; // Seamless fallback
        }
        throw e;
      }
    }
    throw new Error('All providers exhausted');
  }
}
SQLite Schema (database/quota_tracking.sql):


CREATE TABLE provider_quotas (
  provider_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  rpm_used INTEGER,
  rpm_limit INTEGER,
  tpm_used INTEGER,
  tpm_limit INTEGER,
  daily_cost_usd REAL,
  daily_budget_usd REAL,
  reset_at TIMESTAMP,
  is_exhausted BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  last_error TEXT
);
P0: Session Guardian Service
New Service: packages/core/src/sessions/SessionGuardian.ts

Manages external CLI harnesses (opencode, superai-cli, codebuff, etc.) with auto-restart:


interface SessionRuntime {
  sessionId: string;
  harnessType: 'hypercode-native' | 'opencode' | 'superai-cli' | 'codex' | 'claude-code';
  process?: ChildProcess;
  worktreePath: string;
  providerChain: FallbackChain;
  autoRestart: boolean;
  supervisorMode: 'single' | 'council' | 'fallback-cycle';
  state: 'running' | 'crashed' | 'paused' | 'recovering';
}

export class SessionGuardian extends EventEmitter {
  private sessions: Map<string, SessionRuntime> = new Map();
  
  async spawnSession(config: SessionConfig): Promise<string> {
    // Spawn in isolated child process with PTY support
    const proc = spawn(config.command, config.args, {
      cwd: config.worktree,
      env: { ...process.env, ...config.env },
      detached: false
    });
    
    // Monitor with heartbeat
    const sessionId = crypto.randomUUID();
    this.sessions.set(sessionId, { ...config, process: proc, state: 'running' });
    
    proc.on('exit', (code) => this.handleCrash(sessionId, code));
    return sessionId;
  }
  
  private async handleCrash(sessionId: string, code: number) {
    const session = this.sessions.get(sessionId);
    if (session?.autoRestart) {
      this.emit('session_crash', { sessionId, code });
      await this.respawnWithBackoff(sessionId);
    }
  }
}

// apps/web/src/components/dashboard/ProviderQuotaCard.tsx
export function ProviderQuotaCard({ providerId }: { providerId: string }) {
  const { data: quota } = api.providers.getQuota.useQuery(providerId);
  const { mutate: connectOAuth } = api.providers.connectOAuth.useMutation();
  
  return (
    <Card className={quota?.isExhausted ? "border-red-500" : "border-green-500"}>
      <CardHeader>
        <div className="flex justify-between">
          <CardTitle>{providerId}</CardTitle>
          {quota?.isOAuth ? (
            <Badge variant="outline">Connected</Badge>
          ) : (
            <Button onClick={() => connectOAuth(providerId)}>Connect</Button>
          )}
        </div>
      </CardHeader>
      <CardContent>
        <div className="space-y-2">
          <QuotaBar label="RPM" used={quota.rpmUsed} limit={quota.rpmLimit} />
          <QuotaBar label="Daily Cost" used={quota.dailyCost} limit={quota.dailyBudget} currency="$" />
          {quota.isExhausted && (
            <Alert variant="destructive">
              <AlertCircle className="h-4 w-4" />
              <AlertDescription>Quota exhausted. Fallback active.</AlertDescription>
            </Alert>
          )}
        </div>
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}

4. Submodule Research & Indexing Pipeline

Tier	Count	Action	Example

Automated Research Subagent (deploy via packages/research):


// packages/research/src/LinkIngestionService.ts
interface ResearchTask {
  url: string;
  priority: number;
  category?: string;
}

export class LinkIngestionService {
  async processLink(task: ResearchTask) {
    // 1. Scrape (lightweight subagent: Gemini Flash)
    const summary = await this.scrapeAndSummarize(task.url);
    
    // 2. Classify
    const category = await this.classifyTool(summary);
    
    // 3. Decision
    if (category.relevance > 8) {
      await this.addAsSubmodule(task.url, summary);
      await this.scaffoldIntegration(summary);
    } else if (category.relevance > 5) {
      await this.indexForReference(summary);
    } else {
      await this.rejectLink(task.url, 'low_relevance');
    }
    
    // 4. Update HYPERCODE_MASTER_INDEX.jsonc
    await this.updateMasterIndex(summary);
  }
}

1. 🏗️ Architecture Decision: TypeScript/Node.js (Confirmed)
Decision: Full-Stack TypeScript with process isolation via worker_threads + child_process.

Rationale:

Factor	TypeScript	Go/Java
MCP SDK Native	✅ Official @modelcontextprotocol/sdk	❌ Requires bindings
Dashboard Unity	✅ Shared types (packages/types)	❌ API contract overhead
Ecosystem	✅ All AI tools TS-first	❌ Integration friction
Development Speed	✅ Rapid iteration	❌ Compile/deploy cycles
Plugin System	✅ Dynamic imports	❌ Static typing limits
Stability Strategy:


┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    MAIN PROCESS (Control Plane)              │
│  Express + tRPC + WebSocket + Event Bus + Registry State    │
└──────────────┬──────────────────────────────┬───────────────┘
               │                              │

3.1 Provider Fallback Engine (packages/core/src/services/ProviderFallbackService.ts)

// packages/core/src/services/ProviderFallbackService.ts
import { EventEmitter } from 'events';
import { ModelProvider, ModelConfig, QuotaStatus } from '../types/providers';
import { Logger } from '../utils/Logger';

export interface FallbackPolicy {
  policyId: string;
  strategy: 'round-robin' | 'cost-optimized' | 'quota-aware' | 'latency-first';
  chain: ModelConfig[];
  onErrors: {
    quota_exhausted: 'fallback_next' | 'retry_then_fallback';
    rate_limited: 'retry_then_fallback' | 'fallback_next';
    provider_down: 'fallback_next';
  };
  budget?: {
    maxCostUsd: number;
    dailyLimit: number;
  };
}

export class ProviderFallbackService extends EventEmitter {
  private providers: ModelProvider[];
  private policies: Map<string, FallbackPolicy> = new Map();
  private quotaStatus: Map<string, QuotaStatus> = new Map();
  private failureCounts: Map<string, number> = new Map();
  private logger: Logger;
  private currentPolicyId: string = 'default';

  constructor(providers: ModelProvider[], defaultPolicy?: FallbackPolicy) {
    super();
    this.providers = providers;
    this.logger = new Logger('ProviderFallbackService');
    this.initializeQuotaTracking();
    if (defaultPolicy) {
      this.policies.set(defaultPolicy.policyId, defaultPolicy);
    }
  }

  private initializeQuotaTracking() {
    this.providers.forEach(p => {
      this.quotaStatus.set(p.id, {
        provider: p.id,
        rpm: { used: 0, limit: p.rpmLimit || Infinity, resetAt: new Date(Date.now() + 60000) },
        tpm: { used: 0, limit: p.tpmLimit || Infinity, resetAt: new Date(Date.now() + 60000) },
        dailyCost: { used: 0, limit: p.dailyBudget || Infinity, resetAt: new Date(Date.now() + 86400000) },
        isExhausted: false,
        lastError: null,
        consecutiveFailures: 0
      });
    });
  }

  public async selectProvider(taskType?: string): Promise<ModelConfig> {
    const policy = this.policies.get(this.currentPolicyId) || this.getDefaultPolicy();
    const availableChain = this.filterExhaustedProviders(policy.chain);

    if (availableChain.length === 0) {
      this.emit('all_providers_exhausted', { timestamp: new Date(), policy: policy.policyId });
      throw new Error('All providers in fallback chain exhausted');
    }

    const selected = availableChain[0];
    this.logger.info(`Selected provider: ${selected.model} (${selected.provider})`);
    return selected;
  }

  private filterExhaustedProviders(chain: ModelConfig[]): ModelConfig[] {
    return chain.filter(config => {
      const status = this.quotaStatus.get(config.provider);
      return status && !status.isExhausted;
    });
  }

  public reportError(providerId: string, error: Error) {
    const status = this.quotaStatus.get(providerId);
    if (!status) return;

    status.consecutiveFailures++;
    status.lastError = error.message;

    const errorType = this.classifyError(error);
    const policy = this.policies.get(this.currentPolicyId)!;
    const action = policy.onErrors[errorType];

    this.logger.warn(`Provider ${providerId} error: ${errorType} → Action: ${action}`);

    if (errorType === 'quota_exhausted' || status.consecutiveFailures >= 3) {
      status.isExhausted = true;
      this.emit('provider_exhausted', { providerId, errorType, timestamp: new Date() });
    }

    this.quotaStatus.set(providerId, status);
    this.emit('provider_error', { providerId, error: error.message, action });
  }

  private classifyError(error: Error): 'quota_exhausted' | 'rate_limited' | 'provider_down' {
    const message = error.message.toLowerCase();
    if (message.includes('quota') || message.includes('limit')) return 'quota_exhausted';
    if (message.includes('rate') || message.includes('429')) return 'rate_limited';
    return 'provider_down';
  }

  public registerPolicy(policy: FallbackPolicy) {
    this.policies.set(policy.policyId, policy);
    this.logger.info(`Registered fallback policy: ${policy.policyId}`);
  }

  public setActivePolicy(policyId: string) {
    if (this.policies.has(policyId)) {
      this.currentPolicyId = policyId;
      this.emit('policy_changed', { policyId });
    }
  }

  public getQuotaDashboard(): Map<string, QuotaStatus> {
    return new Map(this.quotaStatus);
  }

  public resetQuota(providerId: string) {
    const status = this.quotaStatus.get(providerId);
    if (status) {
      status.isExhausted = false;
      status.consecutiveFailures = 0;
      status.lastError = null;
      this.quotaStatus.set(providerId, status);
      this.emit('quota_reset', { providerId });
    }
  }

  private getDefaultPolicy(): FallbackPolicy {
    return {
      policyId: 'default',
      strategy: 'quota-aware',
      chain: this.providers.map(p => ({
        provider: p.id,
        model: p.defaultModel,
        priority: 1
      })),
      onErrors: {
        quota_exhausted: 'fallback_next',
        rate_limited: 'retry_then_fallback',
        provider_down: 'fallback_next'
      }
    };
  }
}
3.2 Session Guardian (packages/core/src/services/SessionGuardian.ts)

// packages/core/src/services/SessionGuardian.ts
import { spawn, ChildProcess, SpawnOptions } from 'child_process';
import { EventEmitter } from 'events';
import { Logger } from '../utils/Logger';
import { SessionConfig, SessionState } from '../types/sessions';

export interface SessionHandle {
  sessionId: string;
  pid: number;
  status: 'running' | 'paused' | 'stopped' | 'crashed';
  startedAt: Date;
  lastHeartbeat: Date;
  worktree?: string;
  repo?: string;
}

export class SessionGuardian extends EventEmitter {
  private activeSessions: Map<string, SessionHandle> = new Map();
  private processMap: Map<string, ChildProcess> = new Map();
  private sessionConfigs: Map<string, SessionConfig> = new Map();
  private logger: Logger;
  private heartbeatInterval: number = 5000;
  private heartbeatTimer: NodeJS.Timeout | null = null;

  constructor() {
    super();
    this.logger = new Logger('SessionGuardian');
    this.startHeartbeatMonitor();
  }

  public startSession(sessionId: string, config: SessionConfig): SessionHandle {
    this.sessionConfigs.set(sessionId, config);
    const handle = this.spawnProcess(sessionId, config);
    this.activeSessions.set(sessionId, handle);
    this.emit('session_started', { sessionId, pid: handle.pid });
    return handle;
  }

  private spawnProcess(sessionId: string, config: SessionConfig): SessionHandle {
    const [cmd, ...args] = config.command.split(' ');
    
    const options: SpawnOptions = {
      env: { ...process.env, ...config.env, HYPERCODE_SESSION_ID: sessionId },
      cwd: config.cwd || process.cwd(),
      stdio: ['pipe', 'pipe', 'pipe'],
      detached: false
    };

    const child = spawn(cmd, args, options);
    this.processMap.set(sessionId, child);

    const handle: SessionHandle = {
      sessionId,
      pid: child.pid!,
      status: 'running',
      startedAt: new Date(),
      lastHeartbeat: new Date(),
      worktree: config.worktree,
      repo: config.repo
    };

    // Stream logs to WebUI
    child.stdout?.on('data', (data) => {
      this.emit('session_log', { sessionId, data: data.toString(), type: 'stdout' });
      handle.lastHeartbeat = new Date();
    });

    child.stderr?.on('data', (data) => {
      this.emit('session_log', { sessionId, data: data.toString(), type: 'stderr' });
      handle.lastHeartbeat = new Date();
    });

    // Handle crash/restart
    child.on('exit', (code, signal) => {
      handle.status = code === 0 ? 'stopped' : 'crashed';
      this.emit('session_exit', { sessionId, code, signal });
      
      if (config.autoRestart && code !== 0) {
        this.logger.warn(`Session ${sessionId} crashed (code ${code}). Restarting...`);
        this.emit('session_restarting', { sessionId, attempt: this.getRestartCount(sessionId) });
        setTimeout(() => this.restartSession(sessionId), config.restartDelay || 2000);
      }
    });

    child.on('error', (err) => {
      this.emit('session_error', { sessionId, error: err.message });
      handle.status = 'crashed';
    });

    return handle;
  }

  public stopSession(sessionId: string): void {
    const child = this.processMap.get(sessionId);
    const handle = this.activeSessions.get(sessionId);
    
    if (child) {
      child.kill('SIGTERM');
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (child.exitCode === null) child.kill('SIGKILL');
      }, 3000);
    }

    if (handle) {
      handle.status = 'stopped';
      this.activeSessions.set(sessionId, handle);
    }

    this.emit('session_stopped', { sessionId });
  }

  public restartSession(sessionId: string): SessionHandle {
    this.stopSession(sessionId);
    const config = this.sessionConfigs.get(sessionId);
    if (config) {
      return this.startSession(sessionId, config);
    }
    throw new Error(`Session config not found for ${sessionId}`);
  }

  public pauseSession(sessionId: string): void {
    const child = this.processMap.get(sessionId);
    if (child) {
      child.kill('SIGSTOP');
      const handle = this.activeSessions.get(sessionId);
      if (handle) {
        handle.status = 'paused';
        this.activeSessions.set(sessionId, handle);
      }
      this.emit('session_paused', { sessionId });
    }
  }

  public resumeSession(sessionId: string): void {
    const child = this.processMap.get(sessionId);
    if (child) {
      child.kill('SIGCONT');
      const handle = this.activeSessions.get(sessionId);
      if (handle) {
        handle.status = 'running';
        this.activeSessions.set(sessionId, handle);
      }
      this.emit('session_resumed', { sessionId });
    }
  }

  public getSessionState(sessionId: string): SessionHandle | undefined {
    return this.activeSessions.get(sessionId);
  }

  public getAllSessions(): SessionHandle[] {
    return Array.from(this.activeSessions.values());
  }

  private startHeartbeatMonitor() {
    this.heartbeatTimer = setInterval(() => {
      const now = new Date();
      for (const [sessionId, handle] of this.activeSessions.entries()) {
        const elapsed = now.getTime() - handle.lastHeartbeat.getTime();
        if (elapsed > 30000 && handle.status === 'running') {
          this.logger.warn(`Session ${sessionId} heartbeat timeout (${elapsed}ms)`);
          this.emit('session_heartbeat_timeout', { sessionId, elapsed });
        }
      }
    }, this.heartbeatInterval);
  }

  private getRestartCount(sessionId: string): number {
    // Track restart attempts for crash loop detection
    return 0; // Implement counter storage
  }

  public dispose() {
    if (this.heartbeatTimer) clearInterval(this.heartbeatTimer);
    for (const sessionId of this.activeSessions.keys()) {
      this.stopSession(sessionId);
    }
  }
}
3.3 WebUI Dashboard Component (apps/web/src/components/dashboard/MissionControlDashboard.tsx)

// apps/web/src/components/dashboard/MissionControlDashboard.tsx
'use client';

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Card, CardHeader, CardTitle, CardContent } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Progress } from '@/components/ui/progress';
import { Activity, Terminal, Server, AlertCircle, RefreshCw, Play, Pause, StopCircle } from 'lucide-react';
import { trpc } from '@/utils/trpc';

interface SystemStats {
  cpu: number;
  ram: number;
  disk: number;
  network: number;
  activeSessions: number;
}

interface Session {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  model: string;
  status: 'running' | 'paused' | 'stopped' | 'crashed';
  uptime: string;
  lastActivity: string;
}

interface ProviderQuota {
  provider: string;
  model: string;
  rpmUsed: number;
  rpmLimit: number;
  tpmUsed: number;
  tpmLimit: number;
  dailyCost: number;
  dailyBudget: number;
  isExhausted: boolean;
}

export function MissionControlDashboard() {
  const [stats, setStats] = useState<SystemStats>({ cpu: 0, ram: 0, disk: 0, network: 0, activeSessions: 0 });
  const [sessions, setSessions] = useState<Session[]>([]);
  const [quotas, setQuotas] = useState<ProviderQuota[]>([]);

  // Real-time WebSocket connection
  useEffect(() => {
    const ws = new WebSocket('ws://localhost:3001/ws/mission-control');
    
    ws.onmessage = (event) => {
      const data = JSON.parse(event.data);
      switch (data.type) {
        case 'stats':
          setStats(data.payload);
          break;
        case 'sessions':
          setSessions(data.payload);
          break;
        case 'quotas':
          setQuotas(data.payload);
          break;
      }
    };

    return () => ws.close();
  }, []);

  // tRPC mutations for session control
  const restartSession = trpc.sessions.restart.useMutation();
  const pauseSession = trpc.sessions.pause.useMutation();
  const stopSession = trpc.sessions.stop.useMutation();

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-4 p-4 bg-slate-950 min-h-screen">
      {/* Row 1: System Health */}
      <Card className="bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 text-white">
        <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
          <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">CPU Usage</CardTitle>
          <Activity className="h-4 w-4 text-green-400" />
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{stats.cpu}%</div>
          <Progress value={stats.cpu} className="mt-2" />
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      <Card className="bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 text-white">
        <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
          <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">RAM Usage</CardTitle>
          <Server className="h-4 w-4 text-blue-400" />
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{stats.ram}%</div>
          <Progress value={stats.ram} className="mt-2" />
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      <Card className="bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 text-white">
        <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
          <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">Active Sessions</CardTitle>
          <Terminal className="h-4 w-4 text-purple-400" />
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{stats.activeSessions}</div>
          <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">Supervised by Guardian</p>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      <Card className="bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 text-white">
        <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
          <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">System Health</CardTitle>
          <Activity className="h-4 w-4 text-emerald-400" />
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold">🟢 Operational</div>
          <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">All services running</p>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      {/* Row 2: Active Sessions */}
      <Card className="col-span-1 md:col-span-2 lg:col-span-2 bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 text-white">
        <CardHeader>
          <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <Terminal className="h-5 w-5" />
            Session Orchestrator
          </CardTitle>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="space-y-2">
            {sessions.map(session => (
              <div key={session.id} className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-slate-800 rounded-lg">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  <Badge variant={session.status === 'running' ? 'default' : session.status === 'crashed' ? 'destructive' : 'secondary'}>
                    {session.status}
                  </Badge>
                  <div>
                    <span className="font-mono text-sm font-medium">{session.name}</span>
                    <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">{session.model} • {session.uptime}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="flex gap-2">
                  <Button size="sm" variant="outline" onClick={() => pauseSession.mutate({ sessionId: session.id })}>
                    <Pause className="h-3 w-3" />
                  </Button>
                  <Button size="sm" variant="outline" onClick={() => restartSession.mutate({ sessionId: session.id })}>
                    <RefreshCw className="h-3 w-3" />
                  </Button>
                  <Button size="sm" variant="outline" onClick={() => stopSession.mutate({ sessionId: session.id })}>
                    <StopCircle className="h-3 w-3" />
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
            {sessions.length === 0 && (
              <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm text-center py-4">No active sessions</p>
            )}
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      {/* Row 2: Provider Quotas */}
      <Card className="col-span-1 md:col-span-2 lg:col-span-2 bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 text-white">
        <CardHeader>
          <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <Server className="h-5 w-5" />
            Provider Quotas
          </CardTitle>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {quotas.map(quota => (
              <div key={quota.provider} className="p-3 bg-slate-800 rounded-lg">
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
                  <span className="font-medium">{quota.provider}</span>
                  {quota.isExhausted ? (
                    <Badge variant="destructive">Exhausted</Badge>
                  ) : (
                    <Badge variant="default">Active</Badge>
                  )}
                </div>
                <div className="space-y-1">
                  <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                    <span>RPM: {quota.rpmUsed}/{quota.rpmLimit}</span>
                    <span>${quota.dailyCost}/${quota.dailyBudget}</span>
                  </div>
                  <Progress value={(quota.rpmUsed / quota.rpmLimit) * 100} className="h-2" />
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
}

main control plane in Node/TypeScript
worker threads for internal planning/orchestration
child processes for crash-prone / external runtimes
Python sidecars only where already justified
Go/Rust only later for proven bottlenecks
MCP treated as an interface layer, not the sole implementation path
automatic provider/model fallback as the immediate P0
dashboard-first exposure of every important capability
Given your repo, your current maturity level, and your actual feature goals, this is the right path.

What the model outputs got right
Across those responses, the strongest common recommendations were:

keep the core in TypeScript
prioritize provider fallback
build a session supervisor
make the WebUI the main control surface
isolate workloads via worker threads + child processes
normalize external tools behind adapters/plugins
create a research/index pipeline instead of doing ad hoc ingestion
stop over-investing in narrow swarm analytics before the core operator experience is excellent
I agree with all of that.

Direct answer to your architecture question
Should Hypercode use Go or Java?
Use TypeScript as the primary architecture.
Because you need:

shared backend/frontend types
fastest feature iteration

Important correction on concurrency
You asked about “each model on a different thread.”

That is close, but the better design is:

Worker threads

policy evaluation
Child processes
Use for:

long-running coding sessions
external CLIs
MCP servers
browser/computer-use runtimes
untrusted tools
sandboxes
Sidecars
Use for:

OCR
heavy RAG/document work
Python-native pipelines
So the abstraction should be:

one runtime = one managed execution container appropriate to workload and risk
not
one model = one raw JS thread
