3.1 Provider Fallback Chain Editor (LIVE)

// apps/web/src/components/providers/FallbackChainEditor.tsx
import { api } from '@/utils/trpc';
import { DragDropContext, Droppable, Draggable } from '@hello-pangea/dnd';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';

export const FallbackChainEditor = () => {
  const { data: chain } = api.providers.getFallbackChain.useQuery();
  const mutateChain = api.providers.updateFallbackChain.useMutation();

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <h3>Quota-Aware Fallback Chain</h3>
      <DragDropContext onDragEnd={handleReorder}>
        <Droppable droppableId="chain">
          {(provided) => (
            <ul {...provided.droppableProps} ref={provided.innerRef}>
              {chain?.map((model, idx) => (
                <Draggable key={model.id} draggableId={model.id} index={idx}>
                  {(provided) => (
                    <li ref={provided.innerRef} {...provided.draggableProps} {...provided.dragHandleProps}>
                      <Badge>{model.provider}:{model.name} ({model.quota.remaining}%)</Badge>
                    </li>
                  )}
                </Draggable>
              ))}
              {provided.placeholder}
            </ul>
          )}
        </Droppable>
      </DragDropContext>
      <details>
        <summary>Policy Docs</summary>
        <ul>
          <li>Quota Exhaust → Next (e.g., Claude → Gemini)</li>
          <li>Rate-Limit → Retry (3x) → Fallback</li>
          <li>Free-Tier Opt: OpenRouter/Copilot First</li>
        </ul>
      </details>
      <Button onClick={() => mutateChain.mutate({ chain })}>Save & Test</Button>
    </div>
  );
};

            </div>
            <details>
              <summary>Auto-Policy</summary>
              <ul>
                <li>Restart: Always (3s delay)</li>
                <li>Supervisor: Council (Arch/Guard/Opt)</li>
                <li>Fallback Prompts: Cycle 5</li>

            </details>
          </CardContent>
        </Card>
      ))}

        <Button className="w-full h-full">+ New Session (Opencode/etc.)</Button>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
};

### `packages/core/src/providers/types.ts`
```ts
export type ProviderId =
  | 'anthropic'
  | 'openai'
  | 'google'
  | 'openrouter'
  | 'copilot'
  | 'xai'
  | 'deepseek'
  | 'mistral'
  | 'local';

export type ProviderErrorKind =
  | 'quota_exhausted'
  | 'rate_limited'
  | 'auth_failed'
  | 'provider_down'
  | 'timeout'
  | 'unknown';

export type FallbackAction =
  | 'fallback_next'
  | 'retry_then_fallback'
  | 'refresh_and_retry'
  | 'skip_provider';

export interface ProviderModelRef {
  provider: ProviderId;
  model: string;
  label?: string;
}

export interface RetryPolicy {
  maxAttempts: number; // e.g. 2
  backoffMs: number;   // e.g. 1500
}

export interface FallbackPolicy {
  id: string;
  strategy: 'quota_aware_capability_first' | 'ordered' | 'latency_first' | 'cost_optimized';
  chain: ProviderModelRef[];
  onErrors: Record<Exclude<ProviderErrorKind, 'unknown'>, FallbackAction>;
  retry: RetryPolicy;
}

export interface QuotaWindow {
  used: number;
  limit: number;
  resetAt: string; // ISO
}

export interface QuotaSnapshot {
  provider: ProviderId;
  rpm: QuotaWindow;
  tpm: QuotaWindow;
  dailyCostUsd: number;
  dailyBudgetUsd: number;
  exhausted: boolean;
  lastError?: ProviderErrorKind;
  cooldownUntil?: string;
}
```

### `packages/core/src/providers/ProviderRouter.ts`
```ts
import { EventEmitter } from 'node:events';
import {
  FallbackPolicy, ProviderErrorKind, ProviderModelRef, QuotaSnapshot
} from './types';

export interface ExecuteInput {
  policyId: string;
  taskType: 'planning' | 'coding' | 'review' | 'research';
  messages: Array<{ role: 'system' | 'user' | 'assistant'; content: string }>;
}

export interface ExecuteResult {
  provider: string;
  model: string;
  outputText: string;
  switchedFrom?: { provider: string; model: string; reason: ProviderErrorKind };
}

export class ProviderRouter extends EventEmitter {
  constructor(
    private readonly getPolicy: (id: string) => FallbackPolicy,
    private readonly getQuotas: () => Promise<Record<string, QuotaSnapshot>>,
    private readonly invokeModel: (ref: ProviderModelRef, input: ExecuteInput) => Promise<ExecuteResult>,
    private readonly classifyError: (err: unknown) => ProviderErrorKind
  ) { super(); }

  async executeWithFallback(input: ExecuteInput): Promise<ExecuteResult> {
    const policy = this.getPolicy(input.policyId);
    const quotas = await this.getQuotas();

    for (const ref of policy.chain) {
      const q = quotas[ref.provider];
      if (q?.exhausted) continue;

      try {
        const res = await this.invokeModel(ref, input);
        this.emit('provider.decision', { type: 'success', provider: ref.provider, model: ref.model });
        return res;
      } catch (err) {
        const kind = this.classifyError(err);
        this.emit('provider.decision', { type: 'error', provider: ref.provider, model: ref.model, kind });

        const action = policy.onErrors[kind] ?? 'fallback_next';
        if (action === 'retry_then_fallback') {
          for (let i = 0; i < policy.retry.maxAttempts; i++) {
            await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, policy.retry.backoffMs * (i + 1)));
            try {
              const res = await this.invokeModel(ref, input);
              return { ...res, switchedFrom: { provider: ref.provider, model: ref.model, reason: kind } };
            } catch { /* continue */ }
          }
        }
        // fallback_next / refresh_and_retry / skip_provider all continue here for now
      }
    }

    throw new Error('All providers exhausted or unavailable');
  }
}
```

### `packages/core/src/sessions/types.ts`
```ts
export type SessionStatus = 'starting' | 'running' | 'paused' | 'crashed' | 'stopped';

export interface SessionConfig {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  harness: 'hypercode-native' | 'opencode' | 'claude-code' | 'codex' | 'gemini-cli' | 'superai-cli' | string;
  cwd: string;
  command: string;
  args: string[];
  env?: Record<string, string>;
  autoRestart: boolean;
  maxRestartsPerHour: number;
}

export interface SessionRuntime {
  id: string;
  pid?: number;
  status: SessionStatus;
  restartCount: number;
  lastExitCode?: number;
  lastActivityAt?: string;
}
```

</details>

### 🚀 Hypercode Council Synthesis Complete: GPT-5.2 Pro Execution Protocol
**Status:** ALIGNED | **Target:** v2.8.2 | **Phase:** 123 (Operator UX) $\rightarrow$ 124 (Memory & RAG Mastery)

Commander, the Council has spoken and the architecture is sealed. We are locked into the **TypeScript-First Cellular Architecture**. Here is your concrete **Target Architecture Spec** and the **Phase 124 Execution Plan**, delivering the exact UI components and mathematical routing necessary to assimilate `mem0`, `supermemory`, and `claude-mem` into a single pane of glass.

---

### 1. Mathematical RAG & Memory Routing

The core of Phase 124 is ensuring our Memory Plugins don't just dump context, but intelligently rerank it to save tokens. We use a hybrid scoring equation combining Semantic Similarity and Time Decay:

Inline, the threshold $T_{min}$ dictates if a memory is injected into the context window. The scoring function for any given memory vector $\vec{m}$ against query vector $\vec{q}$ is:

$$Score = \left( \frac{ \vec{q} \cdot \vec{m} }{ \|\vec{q}\| \|\vec{m}\| } \right) \cdot e^{-\lambda \Delta t} + \gamma \cdot C_{usage}$$

Where:
*   $\Delta t$ is the age of the memory.
*   $\lambda$ is the recency decay factor.
*   $C_{usage}$ is the historical access frequency (how often this memory was useful).

If $Score > 0.85$, it is automatically injected into the `SessionGuardian`'s active worktree.

<details>
<summary><strong>🧠 View <code>HybridMemoryRouter.ts</code> (The Engine)</strong></summary>

```typescript
// packages/memory/src/HybridMemoryRouter.ts
import { Logger } from '@hypercode/telemetry';
import { db } from '@hypercode/database';

export class HybridMemoryRouter {
  private logger = new Logger('MemoryRouter');

  async retrieveAndRank(query: string, limit: number = 5) {
    // 1. Generate query embedding
    const queryVector = await getEmbedding(query);
    
    // 2. Fetch from active backends (Chroma, pgvector) via Plugins
    const rawMemories = await Promise.all([
      this.plugins.get('pgvector').search(queryVector),
      this.plugins.get('chromadb').search(queryVector)
    ]).then(res => res.flat());

    // 3. Apply hybrid scoring math
    const ranked = rawMemories.map(mem => {
      const timeDecay = Math.exp(-0.01 * mem.ageInDays);
      const score = (mem.cosineSim * timeDecay) + (0.1 * mem.usageCount);
      return { ...mem, finalScore: score };
    });

    // 4. Sort and prune
    return ranked
      .sort((a, b) => b.finalScore - a.finalScore)
      .slice(0, limit);
  }
}
```
</details>

### 3. The Definitive Package Sub-Architecture (The "Cellular" Map)

To ensure your 932+ submodules and plugins do not turn the monorepo into spaghetti, we adhere strictly to this integration contract. Do not place tool code inside `agents`; keep it explicitly isolated.

| Subsystem Package | Protocol layer | Execution Mode | Crash Impact |
| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |
| `packages/core` | TRPC / WebSocket | Main Event Loop | FATAL (System restart via `systemd`/`docker`) |
| `packages/agents` | SharedArrayBuffer | Node `worker_threads`| Thread dies. Overarching OS lives. |
| `packages/sessions`| `stdio` / PTY | `child_process` hooks | Process dies. `SessionGuardian` respawns it. |
| `packages/mcp` | SSE / JSON-RPC | Proxied Middleware | Connection drops. Router falls back. |
| `packages/research`| Background Cron | Node `worker_threads`| Ignored. Auto-retries next cron tick. |

### Next Immediate Actions to Close The Loop:

1. **Deploy the Hybrid Router:** Add the math and embedding logic to `packages/memory/src/HybridMemoryRouter.ts`.
2. **Mount the UI:** Add `/memory` and `/research` routes to the Next.js `apps/web/src/app` directory. 
3. **Execute the Assimilator:** Run the subagent script on the remaining 252 "Redundant" Tier 5 links to explicitly tag them in `rejected_links.txt` so the system stops scanning them.

*"The fleet is ready. We have achieved feature cohesion."* Proceed with Phase 124.

## The Five Concrete Deliverables (In Order)

### Deliverable 1: `FallbackOrchestrator` + `QuotaTracker`

**Location:** `packages/ai/src/fallback/`

```typescript
// packages/ai/src/fallback/types.ts
export interface FallbackPolicy {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  strategy: 'ordered' | 'quota-aware' | 'cost-optimized' | 'latency-first';
  chain: ProviderModelEntry[];
  onErrors: {
    quota_exhausted: 'fallback_next';
    rate_limited: 'retry_then_fallback';
    auth_failure: 'skip_provider';
    provider_down: 'fallback_next';
    timeout: 'retry_same';
  };
  preferences: {
    preferFreeFirst: boolean;
    preferSubscriptionBeforeAPI: boolean;
  };
  budget?: { maxDailyCostUsd: number; maxMonthlyCostUsd: number };
}

export interface ProviderModelEntry {
  providerId: string;       // 'anthropic' | 'google' | 'openai' | ...
  model: string;            // 'claude-opus-4' | 'gemini-2.5-pro' | ...
  authMethod: 'api-key' | 'oauth' | 'free' | 'local';
}

export interface QuotaState {
  providerId: string;
  rpm: { used: number; limit: number; resetAt: Date };
  tpm: { used: number; limit: number; resetAt: Date };
  dailyCost: { used: number; budget: number };
  isExhausted: boolean;
  cooldownUntil?: Date;
  consecutiveFailures: number;
}
```

```typescript
// packages/ai/src/fallback/orchestrator.ts
import { EventEmitter } from 'events';

export class FallbackOrchestrator extends EventEmitter {
  private quotas: Map<string, QuotaState>;
  private policies: Map<string, FallbackPolicy>;
  
  async execute(task: AgenticTask, policyId = 'default'): Promise<ModelResponse> {
    const policy = this.policies.get(policyId)!;
    
    for (const entry of policy.chain) {
      const quota = this.quotas.get(entry.providerId);
      
      // Skip exhausted
      if (quota?.isExhausted) {
        this.emit('provider:skipped', { provider: entry.providerId, reason: 'exhausted' });
        continue;
      }
      if (quota?.cooldownUntil && quota.cooldownUntil > new Date()) {
        this.emit('provider:skipped', { provider: entry.providerId, reason: 'cooldown' });
        continue;
      }
      
      try {
        const response = await this.callProvider(entry, task);
        this.trackSuccess(entry, response);
        return response;
      } catch (err) {
        const action = this.classifyAndAct(err, entry, policy);
        
        if (action === 'retry_then_fallback') {
          const retry = await this.retryWithBackoff(entry, task, 2);
          if (retry) return retry;
        }
        // All other actions: continue to next in chain
        continue;
      }
    }
    
    throw new AllProvidersExhaustedError(policy.chain, this.quotas);
  }
  
  private classifyAndAct(err: any, entry: ProviderModelEntry, policy: FallbackPolicy): string {
    const code = err?.status || err?.code || '';
    const msg = (err?.message || '').toLowerCase();
    
    if (code === 429 || msg.includes('rate limit')) {
      this.setCooldown(entry.providerId, 60_000);
      return policy.onErrors.rate_limited;
    }
    if (code === 402 || msg.includes('quota') || msg.includes('insufficient')) {
      this.markExhausted(entry.providerId);
      return policy.onErrors.quota_exhausted;
    }
    if (code === 401 || code === 403) {
      return policy.onErrors.auth_failure;
    }
    
    this.incrementFailures(entry.providerId);
    return policy.onErrors.provider_down;
  }
}
```

**tRPC Router:**

```typescript
// packages/core/src/routers/providerRouter.ts
export const providerRouter = router({
  quotaStatus: publicProcedure.query(({ ctx }) => {
    return ctx.fallbackOrchestrator.getAllQuotas();
  }),
  
  fallbackChain: publicProcedure.query(({ ctx }) => {
    return ctx.fallbackOrchestrator.getPolicy('default');
  }),
  
  updateFallbackChain: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ policyId: z.string(), chain: z.array(ProviderModelEntrySchema) }))
    .mutation(({ ctx, input }) => {
      return ctx.fallbackOrchestrator.updatePolicy(input.policyId, input.chain);
    }),
    
  connectOAuth: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ providerId: z.string() }))
    .mutation(({ ctx, input }) => {
      return ctx.oauthService.initiateFlow(input.providerId);
    }),
});
```

### Deliverable 2: `SessionSupervisor`

**Location:** `packages/core/src/sessions/`

```typescript
// packages/core/src/sessions/supervisor.ts
import { spawn, ChildProcess } from 'child_process';
import { EventEmitter } from 'events';

interface SessionRuntime {
  id: string;
  harness: string;        // 'hypercode-native' | 'opencode' | 'claude-code' | ...
  cwd: string;
  status: 'starting' | 'running' | 'paused' | 'crashed' | 'stopped';
  autoRestart: boolean;
  restartCount: number;
  maxRestarts: number;
  pid?: number;
  startedAt?: Date;
  lastActivityAt?: Date;
  process?: ChildProcess;  // not serialized
}

const HARNESS_COMMANDS: Record<string, (cwd: string) => { bin: string; args: string[] }> = {
  'hypercode-native': (cwd) => ({ bin: 'node', args: ['packages/cli/dist/index.js', '--dir', cwd] }),
  'opencode':    (cwd) => ({ bin: 'opencode', args: ['--dir', cwd] }),
  'claude-code': (cwd) => ({ bin: 'claude', args: ['--dir', cwd] }),
  'codex':       (cwd) => ({ bin: 'codex', args: [cwd] }),
  'gemini-cli':  (cwd) => ({ bin: 'gemini', args: ['--dir', cwd] }),
  'superai-cli': (cwd) => ({ bin: 'superai', args: ['--dir', cwd] }),
};

export class SessionSupervisor extends EventEmitter {
  private sessions = new Map<string, SessionRuntime>();
  
  async start(config: { id?: string; harness: string; cwd: string; autoRestart?: boolean }): Promise<SessionRuntime> {
    const session: SessionRuntime = {
      id: config.id || crypto.randomUUID(),
      harness: config.harness,
      cwd: config.cwd,
      status: 'starting',
      autoRestart: config.autoRestart ?? true,
      restartCount: 0,
      maxRestarts: 10,
    };
    this.sessions.set(session.id, session);
    await this.spawn(session);
    return session;
  }
  
  private async spawn(session: SessionRuntime) {
    const cmdFn = HARNESS_COMMANDS[session.harness] || 
      ((cwd: string) => ({ bin: session.harness, args: ['--dir', cwd] }));
    const { bin, args } = cmdFn(session.cwd);
    
    const proc = spawn(bin, args, {
      cwd: session.cwd,
      stdio: ['pipe', 'pipe', 'pipe'],
      env: { ...process.env, HYPERCODE_SESSION_ID: session.id },
    });
    
    session.process = proc;
    session.pid = proc.pid;
    session.status = 'running';
    session.startedAt = new Date();
    
    proc.stdout?.on('data', (d) => {
      session.lastActivityAt = new Date();
      this.emit('output', { sessionId: session.id, data: d.toString(), stream: 'stdout' });
    });
    proc.stderr?.on('data', (d) => {
      this.emit('output', { sessionId: session.id, data: d.toString(), stream: 'stderr' });
    });
    
    proc.on('exit', (code) => {
      session.status = code === 0 ? 'stopped' : 'crashed';
      session.process = undefined;
      this.emit('exit', { sessionId: session.id, code });
      
      if (session.autoRestart && code !== 0 && session.restartCount < session.maxRestarts) {
        session.restartCount++;
        const delay = Math.min(1000 * Math.pow(2, session.restartCount - 1), 30000);
        this.emit('restarting', { sessionId: session.id, delay, attempt: session.restartCount });
        setTimeout(() => this.spawn(session), delay);
      } else if (session.restartCount >= session.maxRestarts) {
        this.emit('crash-loop', { sessionId: session.id });
      }
    });
  }
  
  stop(id: string) {
    const s = this.sessions.get(id);
    if (s?.process) { s.process.kill(); s.autoRestart = false; s.status = 'stopped'; }
  }
  
  restart(id: string) {
    this.stop(id);
    const s = this.sessions.get(id);
    if (s) { s.restartCount = 0; s.autoRestart = true; this.spawn(s); }
  }
  
  broadcast(message: string) {
    for (const s of this.sessions.values()) {
      if (s.status === 'running' && s.process?.stdin) {
        s.process.stdin.write(message + '\n');
      }
    }
  }
  
  list(): Omit<SessionRuntime, 'process'>[] {
    return [...this.sessions.values()].map(({ process, ...rest }) => rest);
  }
}
```

**tRPC Router:**

```typescript
// packages/core/src/routers/sessionRouter.ts
export const sessionRouter = router({
  list: publicProcedure.query(({ ctx }) => ctx.sessionSupervisor.list()),
  
  start: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ harness: z.string(), cwd: z.string(), autoRestart: z.boolean().optional() }))
    .mutation(({ ctx, input }) => ctx.sessionSupervisor.start(input)),
    
  stop: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
    .mutation(({ ctx, input }) => ctx.sessionSupervisor.stop(input.id)),
    
  restart: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.string() }))
    .mutation(({ ctx, input }) => ctx.sessionSupervisor.restart(input.id)),
    
  broadcast: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ message: z.string() }))
    .mutation(({ ctx, input }) => ctx.sessionSupervisor.broadcast(input.message)),
});
```

### Deliverable 3: Dashboard Overview Page

```tsx
// apps/web/src/app/page.tsx (or apps/web/src/app/overview/page.tsx)
'use client';

import { api } from '@/utils/trpc';

export default function OverviewPage() {
  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-4 p-6 bg-slate-950 min-h-screen text-white">
      <SystemHealthStrip />
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
        <ActiveSessionsCard />
        <ProviderQuotaCard />
      </div>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
        <MCPHealthCard />
        <MemoryStatsCard />
        <ToolStatusCard />
      </div>
      <RecentActivityFeed />
    </div>
  );
}

function SystemHealthStrip() {
  const { data } = api.system.health.useQuery(undefined, { refetchInterval: 2000 });
  if (!data) return null;
  
  return (
    <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3 p-3 bg-slate-900/50 rounded-lg border border-slate-700">
      {[
        { label: 'CPU', value: data.cpu, unit: '%', warn: 80 },
        { label: 'RAM', value: data.ram, unit: '%', warn: 85 },
        { label: 'GPU', value: data.gpu, unit: '%', warn: 90 },
        { label: 'Disk', value: data.disk, unit: '%', warn: 90 },
        { label: 'Sessions', value: data.activeSessions, unit: '', warn: Infinity },
        { label: 'MCP', value: data.mcpServers, unit: ' servers', warn: Infinity },
        { label: 'Memory', value: data.memoryCount, unit: ' entries', warn: Infinity },
      ].map(m => (
        <div key={m.label} className="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1 bg-slate-800 rounded">
          <span className="text-xs text-slate-400">{m.label}</span>
          <span className={`font-mono font-bold ${
            m.value > m.warn ? 'text-red-400' : 'text-green-400'
          }`}>
            {m.value}{m.unit}
          </span>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

function ProviderQuotaCard() {
  const { data: quotas } = api.providers.quotaStatus.useQuery(undefined, { refetchInterval: 5000 });
  const { data: chain } = api.providers.fallbackChain.useQuery();
  
  return (
    <div className="bg-slate-900 rounded-lg border border-slate-700 p-4">
      <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-3">
        <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Provider Quotas</h2>
        <a href="/providers" className="text-xs text-blue-400 hover:underline">Manage →</a>
      </div>
      {chain && (
        <p className="text-xs text-slate-500 mb-3">
          Chain: {chain.chain.map(c => `${c.providerId}:${c.model}`).join(' → ')}
        </p>
      )}
      <div className="space-y-2">
        {quotas?.map(q => {
          const pct = q.rpm.limit > 0 ? (q.rpm.used / q.rpm.limit) * 100 : 0;
          return (
            <div key={q.providerId} className="space-y-1">
              <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                <span>{q.providerId} {q.isExhausted && '🔴'}</span>
                <span className="text-slate-400">{q.rpm.used}/{q.rpm.limit} RPM</span>
              </div>
              <div className="h-1.5 bg-slate-700 rounded-full">
                <div 
                  className={`h-full rounded-full ${
                    pct > 90 ? 'bg-red-500' : pct > 70 ? 'bg-yellow-500' : 'bg-green-500'
                  }`}
                  style={{ width: `${Math.min(pct, 100)}%` }}
                />
              </div>
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function ActiveSessionsCard() {
  const { data: sessions } = api.sessions.list.useQuery(undefined, { refetchInterval: 3000 });
  const restart = api.sessions.restart.useMutation();
  
  return (
    <div className="bg-slate-900 rounded-lg border border-slate-700 p-4">
      <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-3">
        <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Active Sessions</h2>
        <a href="/sessions" className="text-xs text-blue-400 hover:underline">View All →</a>
      </div>
      <div className="space-y-2">
        {sessions?.slice(0, 5).map(s => (
          <div key={s.id} className="flex items-center justify-between p-2 bg-slate-800 rounded">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <span className={`h-2 w-2 rounded-full ${
                s.status === 'running' ? 'bg-green-400' : 
                s.status === 'crashed' ? 'bg-red-400' : 'bg-yellow-400'
              }`} />
              <span className="font-mono text-sm truncate max-w-[200px]">{s.cwd}</span>
              <span className="text-xs text-slate-500">{s.harness}</span>
            </div>
            <button 
              onClick={() => restart.mutate({ id: s.id })}
              className="text-xs px-2 py-1 bg-slate-700 rounded hover:bg-slate-600"
            >
              ↻
            </button>
          </div>
        ))}
        {(!sessions || sessions.length === 0) && (
          <p className="text-sm text-slate-500 text-center py-4">No active sessions</p>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

```typescript
export interface ResearchItem {
```

## Definition of Done (Hard Gate)

Before declaring Phase 122 complete:

- [ ] Simulated 429 on active task → model switches seamlessly, session continues

## Governance: What Changes Now

1. **Swarm Governance frozen.** Phases 100-121 are complete and parked. No more facet analytics until core operator UX ships.

2. **Fork dependencies eliminated.** `robertpelloni/metamcp` and `robertpelloni/jules-autopilot` functionality lives in `packages/core`. Submodules point to upstream parents only.

3. **Dashboard = primary interface.** Every new backend capability must have a corresponding UI representation before it's considered "done."

4. **Research pipeline is a real subsystem**, not ad-hoc. `packages/research/` manages the 932+ submodule index with structured stages: discover → classify → enrich → decide → emit.

5. **MCP is one mode, not the only mode.** Every capability supports: native → wrapped → process → MCP-exposed → UI-managed.

## 1. Executive Decision: The Cellular TypeScript OS

**Decision**: Pure TypeScript/Node.js with **Cellular Process Isolation**.

**Architecture Topology**:
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    CONTROL PLANE (Main Process)                 │
│  packages/core                                                  │
│  • Express/tRPC/WebSocket API                                   │
│  • ProviderRouter & FallbackPolicyEngine                        │
│  • SessionRuntimeRegistry                                       │
│  • EventBus & Configuration                                     │
└──────────────┬──────────────────────────────┬───────────────────┘
               │                              │
    ┌──────────▼──────────┐      ┌───────────▼────────────┐
    │   AGENT WORKERS     │      │   SESSION RUNTIMES     │
    │   (Worker Threads)  │      │   (Child Processes)    │
    │  • Isolated v8 ctx  │      │  • External CLIs       │
    │  • Model inference  │      │  • MCP Servers         │
    │  • Planning/Ranking │      │  • Browser automation  │
    │  • Crash isolation  │      │  • Code sandboxes      │
    └──────────┬──────────┘      └───────────┬────────────┘
               │                              │
    ┌──────────▼──────────────────────────────▼────────────┐
    │              REDIS MESH BUS (Pub/Sub)              │
    │   • Cross-cell state sync                            │
    │   • Artifact federation                              │
    └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**Crash Boundaries**:
- **Level 1**: Try/catch (tool errors)
- **Level 2**: Worker termination + respawn (model crashes)
- **Level 3**: Process restart + session recovery (CLI/MCP crashes)
- **Level 4**: Circuit breakers (quota exhaustion)

---

## 2. P0 Critical Implementation: The Fallback Engine

**New Service**: `packages/core/src/providers/FallbackPolicyEngine.ts`

This is the **#1 unblocker** for autonomous operation. When Claude hits a 429, Hypercode seamlessly switches to Gemini, then DeepSeek, then local models without user intervention.

```typescript
// packages/core/src/providers/FallbackPolicyEngine.ts
import { EventEmitter } from 'events';
import { Database } from 'better-sqlite3';

interface QuotaStatus {
  providerId: string;
  rpmUsed: number; rpmLimit: number;
  tpmUsed: number; tpmLimit: number;
  dailyCost: number; dailyBudget: number;
  isExhausted: boolean;
  resetAt: Date;
}

interface FallbackPolicy {
  policyId: string;
  strategy: 'quota-aware' | 'cost-optimized' | 'latency-first' | 'capability-match';
  chain: ProviderModelPair[];
  onErrors: {
    quota_exhausted: 'fallback_next' | 'wait_and_retry';
    rate_limited: 'retry_then_fallback' | 'fallback_next';
  };
  budget?: { maxDailyCostUsd: number };
}

export class FallbackPolicyEngine extends EventEmitter {
  private db: Database;
  private policies: Map<string, FallbackPolicy> = new Map();
  
  constructor(dbPath: string) {
    super();
    this.db = new Database(dbPath);
    this.initSchema();
  }

  private initSchema() {
    this.db.exec(`
      CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS provider_quotas (
        provider_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
        rpm_used INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        rpm_limit INTEGER,
        tpm_used INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        tpm_limit INTEGER,
        daily_cost_usd REAL DEFAULT 0,
        daily_budget_usd REAL,
        reset_at TIMESTAMP,
        is_exhausted BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
        last_error TEXT
      );
      
      CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS fallback_events (
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        session_id TEXT,
        from_provider TEXT,
        to_provider TEXT,
        reason TEXT,
        timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
      );
    `);
  }

  public async executeWithFallback(
    task: AgenticTask, 
    policyId: string = 'default'
  ): AsyncIterable<StreamChunk> {
    const policy = this.policies.get(policyId) || this.getDefaultPolicy();
    
    for (const pair of policy.chain) {
      const quota = this.getQuota(pair.providerId);
      
      if (quota.isExhausted || quota.rpmUsed >= quota.rpmLimit) {
        this.emit('provider_skipped', { provider: pair.providerId, reason: 'exhausted' });
        continue;
      }
      
      try {
        const stream = await this.execute(task, pair);
        this.trackUsage(pair, task);
        return stream;
      } catch (e) {
        const action = this.classifyError(e, policy);
        this.emit('provider_error', { 
          provider: pair.providerId, 
          error: e.code, 
          action 
        });
        
        if (e.code === 'QUOTA_EXHAUSTED') {
          this.markExhausted(pair.providerId);
          continue; // Seamless fallback
        }
        
        if (action === 'retry_then_fallback') {
          const retry = await this.retryWithBackoff(pair, task, 2);
          if (retry) return retry;
        }
      }
    }
    
    throw new Error('All providers in fallback chain exhausted');
  }

  private markExhausted(providerId: string) {
    this.db.prepare(`
      UPDATE provider_quotas 
      SET is_exhausted = TRUE, last_error = ?
      WHERE provider_id = ?
    `).run('QUOTA_EXHAUSTED', providerId);
    
    this.emit('provider_exhausted', { providerId, timestamp: new Date() });
  }

  public getQuota(providerId: string): QuotaStatus {
    return this.db.prepare('SELECT * FROM provider_quotas WHERE provider_id = ?')
      .get(providerId) as QuotaStatus;
  }

  public updateQuota(
    providerId: string, 
    usage: { rpm?: number; tpm?: number; cost?: number }
  ) {
    const current = this.getQuota(providerId);
    const newCost = current.dailyCost + (usage.cost || 0);
    
    this.db.prepare(`
      UPDATE provider_quotas 
      SET rpm_used = rpm_used + ?, tpm_used = tpm_used + ?, daily_cost_usd = ?
      WHERE provider_id = ?
    `).run(usage.rpm || 0, usage.tpm || 0, newCost, providerId);
  }
}
```

## 3. P0 Critical Implementation: Session Guardian

**New Service**: `packages/core/src/sessions/SessionGuardian.ts`

Manages external CLI harnesses (opencode, superai-cli, claude-code, codex) with auto-restart and crash loop detection.

```typescript
// packages/core/src/sessions/SessionGuardian.ts
import { spawn, ChildProcess } from 'child_process';
import { EventEmitter } from 'events';
import { FallbackPolicyEngine } from '../providers/FallbackPolicyEngine';

interface SessionRuntime {
  sessionId: string;
  harnessType: 'hypercode-native' | 'opencode' | 'superai-cli' | 'codex' | 'claude-code';
  process?: ChildProcess;
  worktreePath: string;
  providerChain: string;
  autoRestart: boolean;
  restartCount: number;
  maxRestarts: number;
  state: 'running' | 'crashed' | 'paused' | 'recovering';
  lastHeartbeat: Date;
}

export class SessionGuardian extends EventEmitter {
  private sessions = new Map<string, SessionRuntime>();
  private restartBackoffMs = 2000;
  private maxBackoffMs = 30000;

  constructor(private fallbackEngine: FallbackPolicyEngine) {
    super();
    this.startHealthCheck();
  }

  public async spawnSession(config: SessionConfig): Promise<string> {
    const sessionId = crypto.randomUUID();
    const runtime: SessionRuntime = {
      sessionId,
      harnessType: config.harness,
      worktreePath: config.worktree,
      providerChain: config.providerPolicy,
      autoRestart: config.autoRestart ?? true,
      restartCount: 0,
      maxRestarts: 10,
      state: 'running',
      lastHeartbeat: new Date()
    };

    await this.startProcess(runtime, config);
    this.sessions.set(sessionId, runtime);
    this.emit('session_started', { sessionId, harness: config.harness });
    
    return sessionId;
  }

  private async startProcess(runtime: SessionRuntime, config: SessionConfig) {
    const cmd = this.resolveCommand(runtime.harnessType, config);
    
    const proc = spawn(cmd.bin, cmd.args, {
      cwd: config.worktree,
      env: { ...process.env, ...config.env, HYPERCODE_SESSION_ID: runtime.sessionId },
      stdio: ['pipe', 'pipe', 'pipe'],
      detached: false
    });

    runtime.process = proc;
    runtime.state = 'running';
    runtime.lastHeartbeat = new Date();

    // Stream stdout/stderr to WebUI via EventBus
    proc.stdout?.on('data', (data) => {
      this.emit('session_output', { 
        sessionId: runtime.sessionId, 
        stream: 'stdout', 
        data: data.toString() 
      });
      runtime.lastHeartbeat = new Date();
    });

    proc.stderr?.on('data', (data) => {
      this.emit('session_output', { 
        sessionId: runtime.sessionId, 
        stream: 'stderr', 
        data: data.toString() 
      });
    });

    proc.on('exit', (code) => {
      runtime.state = code === 0 ? 'stopped' : 'crashed';
      this.emit('session_exit', { sessionId: runtime.sessionId, code });
      
      if (runtime.autoRestart && code !== 0) {
        this.handleCrash(runtime);
      }
    });
  }

  private async handleCrash(runtime: SessionRuntime) {
    runtime.restartCount++;
    
    if (runtime.restartCount >= runtime.maxRestarts) {
      this.emit('crash_loop_detected', { sessionId: runtime.sessionId });
      runtime.state = 'stopped';
      return;
    }

    const backoff = Math.min(
      this.restartBackoffMs * Math.pow(2, runtime.restartCount - 1),
      this.maxBackoffMs
    );

    this.emit('session_restarting', { 
      sessionId: runtime.sessionId, 
      attempt: runtime.restartCount,
      backoffMs: backoff 
    });

    setTimeout(() => {
      runtime.state = 'recovering';
      // Re-fetch config and restart
      const config = this.getSessionConfig(runtime.sessionId);
      this.startProcess(runtime, config);
    }, backoff);
  }

  public broadcastToAll(message: string) {
    for (const [id, session] of this.sessions) {
      if (session.state === 'running' && session.process?.stdin) {
        session.process.stdin.write(message + '\n');
      }
    }
  }

  private startHealthCheck() {
    setInterval(() => {
      const now = Date.now();
      for (const [id, session] of this.sessions.entries()) {
        if (session.state === 'running' && (now - session.lastHeartbeat.getTime()) > 60000) {
          this.emit('session_heartbeat_timeout', { sessionId: id });
          // Force restart if unresponsive
          session.process?.kill();
          this.handleCrash(session);
        }
      }
    }, 10000);
  }
}
```

```typescript
// apps/web/src/components/dashboard/SystemHealthStrip.tsx
export function SystemHealthStrip() {

  });

  return (
```

```typescript
// apps/web/src/components/dashboard/ProviderMatrix.tsx
export function ProviderMatrix() {
  const { data: providers } = api.providers.list.useQuery();
  const { data: chain } = api.providers.getFallbackChain.useQuery();
  const updateChain = api.providers.updateFallbackChain.useMutation();

  return (
    <Card className="bg-slate-900 border-slate-700">
      <CardHeader>
        <CardTitle>Provider Fallback Chain</CardTitle>
        <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">
          Drag to reorder. System automatically falls back on quota exhaustion.
        </p>
      </CardHeader>
      <CardContent>
        <div className="space-y-2">
          {chain?.map((model, idx) => (
            <div key={model.id} className="flex items-center gap-4 p-2 bg-slate-800 rounded">
              <span className="text-slate-400">#{idx + 1}</span>
              <ProviderIcon id={model.provider} />
              <span className="font-mono">{model.name}</span>
              <QuotaBar 
                used={model.quotaUsed} 
                limit={model.quotaLimit} 
              />
              {model.isExhausted && (
                <Badge variant="destructive">Exhausted</Badge>
              )}
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
        
        <div className="mt-4 space-y-2">
          <h4 className="text-sm font-medium">OAuth Connections</h4>
          <div className="flex gap-2">
            <OAuthButton provider="anthropic" label="Claude Max" />
            <OAuthButton provider="google" label="AI Plus" />
            <OAuthButton provider="github" label="Copilot Premium" />
            <OAuthButton provider="opencode" label="OpenCode Black" />
          </div>
        </div>
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}
```

### 4.3 Session Supervisor Grid

```typescript
// apps/web/src/components/dashboard/SessionGrid.tsx
export function SessionSupervisor() {
  const { data: sessions } = api.sessions.list.useQuery();
  const restart = api.sessions.restart.useMutation();
  const broadcast = api.sessions.broadcast.useMutation();

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
        <h2 className="text-xl font-bold text-white">Active Sessions</h2>
        <Button onClick={() => broadcast.mutate({ message: 'System broadcast' })}>
          Broadcast to All
        </Button>
      </div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
        {sessions?.map(session => (
          <SessionCard 
            key={session.id} 
            session={session}
            onRestart={() => restart.mutate({ id: session.id })}
          />
        ))}
        
        <NewSessionButton />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function SessionCard({ session, onRestart }: { session: Session, onRestart: () => void }) {
  const [showTerminal, setShowTerminal] = useState(false);
  
  return (
    <Card className={`bg-slate-900 border-slate-700 ${
      session.status === 'crashed' ? 'border-red-500' : ''
    }`}>
      <CardHeader className="pb-2">
        <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
          <div>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <StatusDot status={session.status} />
              <span className="font-mono text-sm">{session.name}</span>
            </div>
            <p className="text-xs text-slate-400 mt-1">
              {session.harness} • {session.model} • 
              Restarts: {session.restartCount}
            </p>
          </div>
          <div className="flex gap-2">
            <Button size="icon" variant="outline" onClick={() => setShowTerminal(!showTerminal)}>
              <Terminal className="h-4 w-4" />
            </Button>
            <Button size="icon" variant="outline" onClick={onRestart}>
              <RotateCw className="h-4 w-4" />
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </CardHeader>
      
      {showTerminal && (
        <CardContent className="pt-0">
          <TerminalEmulator sessionId={session.id} />
        </CardContent>
      )}
    </Card>
  );
}
```

## 2. 🏗️ Consolidated Architecture Decision

### 2.1 Language & Runtime Strategy

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    CONTROL PLANE (Main Process)                  │
│  packages/core — Express + tRPC + WebSocket + Event Bus         │
│  • ProviderRouter & FallbackPolicyEngine                        │
│  • SessionRuntimeRegistry                                       │
│  • Configuration/Auth/Secrets                                   │
│  • Dashboard API (never does heavy compute)                     │
└──────────────┬──────────────────────────────┬───────────────────┘
               │                              │
    ┌──────────▼──────────┐      ┌───────────▼────────────┐
    │   WORKER THREADS    │      │   CHILD PROCESSES      │
    │   (Agent Logic)     │      │   (Session Runtimes)   │
    │  • Prompt planning  │      │  • External CLIs       │
    │  • Context ranking  │      │  • MCP Servers         │
    │  • Tool selection   │      │  • Browser automation  │
    │  • Crash isolation  │      │  • Code sandboxes      │
    └─────────────────────┘      └────────────────────────┘
```

**Decision:** **Full-Stack TypeScript** with process isolation via `worker_threads` + `child_process`.

**Rationale:**
| Factor | TypeScript | Go/Java |
|--------|------------|---------|
| MCP SDK Native | ✅ Official `@modelcontextprotocol/sdk` | ❌ Requires bindings |
| Dashboard Unity | ✅ Shared types (`packages/types`) | ❌ API contract overhead |
| Ecosystem | ✅ All AI tools TS-first | ❌ Integration friction |
| Development Speed | ✅ Rapid iteration | ❌ Compile/deploy cycles |
| Plugin System | ✅ Dynamic imports | ❌ Static typing limits |

## 4. 💻 Core Implementation Scaffolding

### 4.1 Provider Fallback Engine (`packages/core/src/providers/FallbackPolicyEngine.ts`)

```typescript
// packages/core/src/providers/FallbackPolicyEngine.ts
import { EventEmitter } from 'events';
import { ModelProvider, ModelConfig, QuotaStatus } from '../types/providers';
import { Logger } from '../utils/Logger';

export interface FallbackPolicy {
  policyId: string;
  strategy: 
    | 'ordered'
    | 'quota-aware'
    | 'cost-optimized'
    | 'latency-first'
    | 'capability-match'
    | 'cost_per_success_then_latency';
  
  chain: ModelConfig[];
  
  onErrors: {
    quota_exhausted: 'fallback_next' | 'wait_and_retry';
    rate_limited: 'retry_then_fallback' | 'fallback_next';
    auth_failure: 'skip_provider' | 'refresh_and_retry';
    provider_down: 'fallback_next';
    timeout: 'retry_same' | 'fallback_next';
  };
  
  budget?: {
    maxDailyCostUsd: number;
    maxMonthlyCostUsd: number;
  };
  
  preferences?: {
    preferFreeFirst: boolean;
    preferSubscriptionBeforeAPI: boolean;
    stayInModelFamily: boolean;
  };
}

export class FallbackPolicyEngine extends EventEmitter {
  private providers: ModelProvider[];
  private policies: Map<string, FallbackPolicy> = new Map();
  private quotaStatus: Map<string, QuotaStatus> = new Map();
  private failureCounts: Map<string, number> = new Map();
  private logger: Logger;
  private currentPolicyId: string = 'default';

  constructor(providers: ModelProvider[], defaultPolicy?: FallbackPolicy) {
    super();
    this.providers = providers;
    this.logger = new Logger('FallbackPolicyEngine');
    this.initializeQuotaTracking();
    if (defaultPolicy) {
      this.policies.set(defaultPolicy.policyId, defaultPolicy);
    }
  }

  private initializeQuotaTracking() {
    this.providers.forEach(p => {
      this.quotaStatus.set(p.id, {
        provider: p.id,
        rpm: { used: 0, limit: p.rpmLimit || Infinity, resetAt: new Date(Date.now() + 60000) },
        tpm: { used: 0, limit: p.tpmLimit || Infinity, resetAt: new Date(Date.now() + 60000) },
        dailyCost: { used: 0, limit: p.dailyBudget || Infinity, resetAt: new Date(Date.now() + 86400000) },
        isExhausted: false,
        lastError: null,
        consecutiveFailures: 0,
        cooldownUntil: undefined
      });
    });
  }

  public async executeWithFallback(task: any, policyId?: string): Promise<any> {
    const policy = this.policies.get(policyId || this.currentPolicyId) || this.getDefaultPolicy();
    const chain = this.resolveChain(policy, task);
    
    for (const provider of chain) {
      const quota = this.quotaStatus.get(provider.provider);
      
      // Skip exhausted/cooling providers
      if (quota?.isExhausted || (quota?.cooldownUntil && quota.cooldownUntil > Date.now())) {
        this.emitTelemetry('skipped', provider, 'exhausted');
        continue;
      }
      
      try {
        const result = await this.callProvider(provider, task);
        this.trackUsage(provider, result);
        this.emitTelemetry('success', provider, result);
        return result;
      } catch (e) {
        const action = this.classifyError(e, policy);
        this.emitTelemetry('error', provider, { error: e.message, action });
        
        if (action === 'retry_then_fallback') {
          const retry = await this.retryWithBackoff(provider, task, 2);
          if (retry) return retry;
        }
        
        if (action === 'fallback_next') continue;
        if (action === 'refresh_and_retry') {
          await this.refreshAuth(provider);
          continue;
        }
      }
    }
    
    throw new Error('All providers in fallback chain exhausted');
  }

  private resolveChain(policy: FallbackPolicy, task: any): ModelConfig[] {
    const chain = [...policy.chain];
    
    // Apply preferences
    if (policy.preferences?.preferFreeFirst) {
      chain.sort((a, b) => (a.isFree ? -1 : 1) - (b.isFree ? -1 : 1));
    }
    
    if (policy.strategy === 'quota-aware') {
      return chain.filter(config => {
        const status = this.quotaStatus.get(config.provider);
        return status && !status.isExhausted;
      });
    }
    
    return chain;
  }

  private classifyError(error: Error, policy: FallbackPolicy): string {
    const message = error.message.toLowerCase();
    if (message.includes('quota') || message.includes('limit')) return 'quota_exhausted';
    if (message.includes('rate') || message.includes('429')) return 'rate_limited';
    if (message.includes('auth') || message.includes('401')) return 'auth_failure';
    if (message.includes('timeout')) return 'timeout';
    return 'provider_down';
  }

  private emitTelemetry(type: string, provider: ModelConfig, data: any) {
    this.emit('provider:decision', {
      type,
      provider: provider.provider,
      model: provider.model,
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      ...data
    });
  }

  private async retryWithBackoff(provider: ModelConfig, task: any, maxAttempts: number): Promise<any> {
    for (let attempt = 1; attempt <= maxAttempts; attempt++) {
      const delay = Math.pow(2, attempt) * 1000; // Exponential backoff
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));
      
      try {
        return await this.callProvider(provider, task);
      } catch (e) {
        if (attempt === maxAttempts) throw e;
      }
    }
  }

  private async refreshAuth(provider: ModelConfig): Promise<void> {
    // Implement OAuth token refresh logic
    this.emit('provider:auth_refreshed', { provider: provider.provider });
  }

  private async callProvider(provider: ModelConfig, task: any): Promise<any> {
    // Actual provider call implementation
    throw new Error('Not implemented');
  }

  private trackUsage(provider: ModelConfig, result: any): void {
    const status = this.quotaStatus.get(provider.provider);
    if (status) {
      status.rpm.used++;
      status.dailyCost.used += result.cost || 0;
      this.quotaStatus.set(provider.provider, status);
    }
  }

  public registerPolicy(policy: FallbackPolicy) {
    this.policies.set(policy.policyId, policy);
    this.logger.info(`Registered fallback policy: ${policy.policyId}`);
  }

  public setActivePolicy(policyId: string) {
    if (this.policies.has(policyId)) {
      this.currentPolicyId = policyId;
      this.emit('policy_changed', { policyId });
    }
  }

  public getQuotaDashboard(): Map<string, QuotaStatus> {
    return new Map(this.quotaStatus);
  }

  public resetQuota(providerId: string) {
    const status = this.quotaStatus.get(providerId);
    if (status) {
      status.isExhausted = false;
      status.consecutiveFailures = 0;
      status.lastError = null;
      status.cooldownUntil = undefined;
      this.quotaStatus.set(providerId, status);
      this.emit('quota_reset', { providerId });
    }
  }

  private getDefaultPolicy(): FallbackPolicy {
    return {
      policyId: 'default',
      strategy: 'quota-aware',
      chain: this.providers.map(p => ({
        provider: p.id,
        model: p.defaultModel,
        priority: 1,
        isFree: p.isFree || false
      })),
      onErrors: {
        quota_exhausted: 'fallback_next',
        rate_limited: 'retry_then_fallback',
        auth_failure: 'refresh_and_retry',
        provider_down: 'fallback_next',
        timeout: 'retry_same'
      },
      preferences: {
        preferFreeFirst: false,
        preferSubscriptionBeforeAPI: true,
        stayInModelFamily: true
      }
    };
  }
}
```

### 4.2 Session Guardian Service (`packages/core/src/sessions/SessionGuardian.ts`)

```typescript
// packages/core/src/sessions/SessionGuardian.ts
import { spawn, ChildProcess, SpawnOptions } from 'child_process';
import { EventEmitter } from 'events';
import { Logger } from '../utils/Logger';
import { SessionConfig, SessionState } from '../types/sessions';

export interface SessionHandle {
  sessionId: string;
  pid: number;
  status: 'running' | 'paused' | 'stopped' | 'crashed';
  startedAt: Date;
  lastHeartbeat: Date;
  worktree?: string;
  repo?: string;
  harness: string;
  restartCount: number;
  crashLoopDetected: boolean;
}

export class SessionGuardian extends EventEmitter {
  private activeSessions: Map<string, SessionHandle> = new Map();
  private processMap: Map<string, ChildProcess> = new Map();
  private sessionConfigs: Map<string, SessionConfig> = new Map();
  private logger: Logger;
  private heartbeatInterval: number = 5000;
  private heartbeatTimer: NodeJS.Timeout | null = null;
  private maxRestartsPerHour: number = 8;
  private crashLoopCooldownMs: number = 60000;

  constructor() {
    super();
    this.logger = new Logger('SessionGuardian');
    this.startHeartbeatMonitor();
  }

  public startSession(sessionId: string, config: SessionConfig): SessionHandle {
    this.sessionConfigs.set(sessionId, config);
    const handle = this.spawnProcess(sessionId, config);
    this.activeSessions.set(sessionId, handle);
    this.emit('session_started', { sessionId, pid: handle.pid });
    return handle;
  }

  private spawnProcess(sessionId: string, config: SessionConfig): SessionHandle {
    const [cmd, ...args] = config.command.split(' ');
    
    const options: SpawnOptions = {
      env: { ...process.env, ...config.env, HYPERCODE_SESSION_ID: sessionId },
      cwd: config.cwd || process.cwd(),
      stdio: ['pipe', 'pipe', 'pipe'],
      detached: false
    };

    const child = spawn(cmd, args, options);
    this.processMap.set(sessionId, child);

    const handle: SessionHandle = {
      sessionId,
      pid: child.pid!,
      status: 'running',
      startedAt: new Date(),
      lastHeartbeat: new Date(),
      worktree: config.worktree,
      repo: config.repo,
      harness: config.harness || 'hypercode-native',
      restartCount: 0,
      crashLoopDetected: false
    };

    // Stream logs to WebUI
    child.stdout?.on('data', (data) => {
      this.emit('session_log', { sessionId, data: data.toString(), type: 'stdout' });
      handle.lastHeartbeat = new Date();
    });

    child.stderr?.on('data', (data) => {
      this.emit('session_log', { sessionId, data: data.toString(), type: 'stderr' });
      handle.lastHeartbeat = new Date();
    });

    // Handle crash/restart
    child.on('exit', (code, signal) => {
      handle.status = code === 0 ? 'stopped' : 'crashed';
      this.emit('session_exit', { sessionId, code, signal });
      
      if (config.autoRestart && code !== 0 && !handle.crashLoopDetected) {
        this.logger.warn(`Session ${sessionId} crashed (code ${code}). Restarting...`);
        this.emit('session_restarting', { sessionId, attempt: handle.restartCount + 1 });
        this.scheduleRestart(sessionId, config);
      }
    });

    child.on('error', (err) => {
      this.emit('session_error', { sessionId, error: err.message });
      handle.status = 'crashed';
    });

    return handle;
  }

  private scheduleRestart(sessionId: string, config: SessionConfig): void {
    const handle = this.activeSessions.get(sessionId);
    if (!handle) return;

    handle.restartCount++;
    
    // Crash loop detection
    if (handle.restartCount >= this.maxRestartsPerHour) {
      handle.crashLoopDetected = true;
      handle.status = 'stopped';
      this.emit('session_crash_loop', { sessionId, restartCount: handle.restartCount });
      this.logger.error(`Session ${sessionId} in crash loop. Stopping.`);
      return;
    }

    // Exponential backoff
    const delay = Math.min(
      (config.restartDelay || 2000) * Math.pow(2, handle.restartCount - 1),
      30000
    );

    setTimeout(() => {
      if (!handle.crashLoopDetected) {
        this.spawnProcess(sessionId, config);
      }
    }, delay);
  }

  public stopSession(sessionId: string): void {
    const child = this.processMap.get(sessionId);
    const handle = this.activeSessions.get(sessionId);
    
    if (child) {
      child.kill('SIGTERM');
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (child.exitCode === null) child.kill('SIGKILL');
      }, 3000);
    }

    if (handle) {
      handle.status = 'stopped';
      this.activeSessions.set(sessionId, handle);
    }

    this.emit('session_stopped', { sessionId });
  }

  public restartSession(sessionId: string): SessionHandle {
    this.stopSession(sessionId);
    const config = this.sessionConfigs.get(sessionId);
    if (config) {
      return this.startSession(sessionId, config);
    }
    throw new Error(`Session config not found for ${sessionId}`);
  }

  public pauseSession(sessionId: string): void {
    const child = this.processMap.get(sessionId);
    if (child) {
      child.kill('SIGSTOP');
      const handle = this.activeSessions.get(sessionId);
      if (handle) {
        handle.status = 'paused';
        this.activeSessions.set(sessionId, handle);
      }
      this.emit('session_paused', { sessionId });
    }
  }

  public resumeSession(sessionId: string): void {
    const child = this.processMap.get(sessionId);
    if (child) {
      child.kill('SIGCONT');
      const handle = this.activeSessions.get(sessionId);
      if (handle) {
        handle.status = 'running';
        this.activeSessions.set(sessionId, handle);
      }
      this.emit('session_resumed', { sessionId });
    }
  }

  public getSessionState(sessionId: string): SessionHandle | undefined {
    return this.activeSessions.get(sessionId);
  }

  public getAllSessions(): SessionHandle[] {
    return Array.from(this.activeSessions.values());
  }

  private startHeartbeatMonitor() {
    this.heartbeatTimer = setInterval(() => {
      const now = new Date();
      for (const [sessionId, handle] of this.activeSessions.entries()) {
        const elapsed = now.getTime() - handle.lastHeartbeat.getTime();
        if (elapsed > 30000 && handle.status === 'running') {
          this.logger.warn(`Session ${sessionId} heartbeat timeout (${elapsed}ms)`);
          this.emit('session_heartbeat_timeout', { sessionId, elapsed });
        }
      }
    }, this.heartbeatInterval);
  }

  public async broadcastToAll(message: string): Promise<void> {
    for (const [sessionId, handle] of this.activeSessions.entries()) {
      if (handle.status === 'running') {
        const child = this.processMap.get(sessionId);
        if (child?.stdin) {
          child.stdin.write(message + '\n');
        }
      }
    }
    this.emit('broadcast_sent', { message, sessionCount: this.activeSessions.size });
  }

  public dispose() {
    if (this.heartbeatTimer) clearInterval(this.heartbeatTimer);
    for (const sessionId of this.activeSessions.keys()) {
      this.stopSession(sessionId);
    }
  }
}
```

### 4.3 WebUI Dashboard Component (`apps/web/src/app/overview/page.tsx`)

```tsx
// apps/web/src/app/overview/page.tsx
'use client';

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Card, CardHeader, CardTitle, CardContent } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Progress } from '@/components/ui/progress';
import { Activity, Terminal, Server, AlertCircle, RefreshCw, Play, Pause, StopCircle, Zap, Brain, Network } from 'lucide-react';
import { trpc } from '@/utils/trpc';

interface SystemStats {
  cpu: number;
  ram: number;
  disk: number;
  network: number;
  activeSessions: number;
  mcpServers: number;
  memoryCount: number;
}

interface Session {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  model: string;
  harness: string;
  status: 'running' | 'paused' | 'stopped' | 'crashed';
  uptime: string;
  lastActivity: string;
  restartCount: number;
}

interface ProviderQuota {
  provider: string;
  model: string;
  rpmUsed: number;
  rpmLimit: number;
  tpmUsed: number;
  tpmLimit: number;
  dailyCost: number;
  dailyBudget: number;
  isExhausted: boolean;
  resetIn?: string;
  authMethod: 'oauth' | 'api_key';
  oauthConnected?: boolean;
}

export default function OverviewPage() {
  const [stats, setStats] = useState<SystemStats>({ 
    cpu: 0, ram: 0, disk: 0, network: 0, 
    activeSessions: 0, mcpServers: 0, memoryCount: 0 
  });
  const [sessions, setSessions] = useState<Session[]>([]);
  const [quotas, setQuotas] = useState<ProviderQuota[]>([]);

  // Real-time WebSocket connection
  useEffect(() => {
    const ws = new WebSocket('ws://localhost:3001/ws/mission-control');
    
    ws.onmessage = (event) => {
      const data = JSON.parse(event.data);
      switch (data.type) {
        case 'stats':
          setStats(data.payload);
          break;
        case 'sessions':
          setSessions(data.payload);
          break;
        case 'quotas':
          setQuotas(data.payload);
          break;
      }
    };

    return () => ws.close();
  }, []);

  // tRPC mutations for session control
  const restartSession = trpc.sessions.restart.useMutation();
  const pauseSession = trpc.sessions.pause.useMutation();
  const stopSession = trpc.sessions.stop.useMutation();

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-4 p-6 bg-slate-950 min-h-screen">
      {/* Row 1: System Vitals Strip */}
      <SystemHealthStrip stats={stats} />
      
      {/* Row 2: Primary Operational Cards */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
        <ActiveSessionsCard sessions={sessions} restartSession={restartSession} pauseSession={pauseSession} stopSession={stopSession} />
        <ProviderQuotaCard quotas={quotas} />
      </div>
      
      {/* Row 3: Infrastructure Status */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
        <MCPServerHealthCard mcpServers={stats.mcpServers} />
        <MemoryStatsCard memoryCount={stats.memoryCount} />
        <ToolInventoryCard />
      </div>
      
      {/* Row 4: Activity Feed + Quick Actions */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
        <div className="lg:col-span-2">
          <RecentActivityFeed />
        </div>
        <QuickActionPanel />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function SystemHealthStrip({ stats }: { stats: SystemStats }) {
  return (
    <div className="flex gap-4 p-3 bg-slate-900/50 rounded-lg border border-slate-700">
      <MetricPill label="CPU" value={stats.cpu} unit="%" color={stats.cpu > 80 ? 'red' : stats.cpu > 50 ? 'yellow' : 'green'} />
      <MetricPill label="RAM" value={stats.ram} unit="%" color={stats.ram > 85 ? 'red' : 'green'} />
      <MetricPill label="Disk" value={stats.disk} unit="%" />
      <MetricPill label="MCP" value={stats.mcpServers} unit=" active" />
      <MetricPill label="Sessions" value={stats.activeSessions} unit=" running" />
      <MetricPill label="Memory" value={stats.memoryCount} unit=" entries" />
    </div>
  );
}

function MetricPill({ label, value, unit, color = 'green' }: { label: string; value: number | string; unit: string; color?: string }) {
  const colorClasses = {
    green: 'text-green-400',
    yellow: 'text-yellow-400',
    red: 'text-red-400'
  };
  
  return (
    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1 bg-slate-800 rounded-full">
      <span className="text-xs text-slate-400">{label}</span>
      <span className={`text-sm font-bold ${colorClasses[color as keyof typeof colorClasses]}`}>
        {value}{unit}
      </span>
    </div>
  );
}

function ActiveSessionsCard({ sessions, restartSession, pauseSession, stopSession }: any) {
  return (
    <Card className="bg-slate-900 border-slate-700">
      <CardHeader>
        <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Terminal className="h-5 w-5 text-purple-400" />
          Active Sessions
        </CardTitle>
      </CardHeader>
      <CardContent className="space-y-2">
        {sessions.map((session: Session) => (
          <div key={session.id} className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-slate-800 rounded-lg">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <Badge variant={session.status === 'running' ? 'default' : session.status === 'crashed' ? 'destructive' : 'secondary'}>
                {session.status}
              </Badge>
              <div>
                <span className="font-mono text-sm font-medium">{session.name}</span>
                <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">{session.harness} • {session.model}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="flex gap-2">
              <Button size="sm" variant="outline" onClick={() => pauseSession.mutate({ sessionId: session.id })}>
                <Pause className="h-3 w-3" />
              </Button>
              <Button size="sm" variant="outline" onClick={() => restartSession.mutate({ sessionId: session.id })}>
                <RefreshCw className="h-3 w-3" />
              </Button>
              <Button size="sm" variant="outline" onClick={() => stopSession.mutate({ sessionId: session.id })}>
                <StopCircle className="h-3 w-3" />
              </Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}

function ProviderQuotaCard({ quotas }: { quotas: ProviderQuota[] }) {
  return (
    <Card className="bg-slate-900 border-slate-700">
      <CardHeader>
        <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Zap className="h-5 w-5 text-yellow-400" />
          Provider Quotas
        </CardTitle>
      </CardHeader>
      <CardContent className="space-y-3">
        {quotas.map(quota => (
          <ProviderQuotaBar key={quota.provider} provider={quota} />
        ))}
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}

function ProviderQuotaBar({ provider }: { provider: ProviderQuota }) {
  const pctUsed = (provider.rpmUsed / provider.rpmLimit) * 100;
  const color = pctUsed > 90 ? 'bg-red-500' : pctUsed > 70 ? 'bg-yellow-500' : 'bg-green-500';
  
  return (
    <div className="space-y-1">
      <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
        <span className="flex items-center gap-2">
          {provider.provider}
          {provider.authMethod === 'oauth' && (
            <Badge variant="outline" className="text-[10px]">
              {provider.oauthConnected ? '✅ Connected' : '⚠️ Not connected'}
            </Badge>
          )}
        </span>
        <span className="text-slate-400">
          {provider.rpmUsed}/{provider.rpmLimit} RPM
          {provider.resetIn && ` • Resets ${provider.resetIn}`}
        </span>
      </div>
      <div className="h-2 bg-slate-700 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
        <div className={`h-full ${color} rounded-full transition-all`} style={{ width: `${pctUsed}%` }} />
      </div>
      {provider.isExhausted && (
        <div className="text-xs text-red-400">⚠️ Quota exhausted — Fallback active</div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

function MCPServerHealthCard({ mcpServers }: { mcpServers: number }) {
  return (
    <Card className="bg-slate-900 border-slate-700">
      <CardHeader>
        <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Network className="h-5 w-5 text-blue-400" />
          MCP Servers
        </CardTitle>
      </CardHeader>
      <CardContent>
        <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{mcpServers}</div>
        <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">Active servers</p>
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}

      <CardHeader>
        <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Brain className="h-5 w-5 text-cyan-400" />
          Memory
        </CardTitle>
      </CardHeader>
      <CardContent>
        <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{memoryCount}</div>

      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}

      <CardHeader>
        <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">

          Tools
        </CardTitle>
      </CardHeader>
      <CardContent>
        <div className="text-2xl font-bold">🟢 Operational</div>
        <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">All systems running</p>
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}

function RecentActivityFeed() {

        <CardTitle>Recent Activity</CardTitle>

        <div className="space-y-2 text-sm text-slate-400">

      </CardHeader>
```

# What is now P0

## P0.1 — Provider fallback
Must exist before broader autonomy is taken seriously.

Build:

- `ProviderRouter`
- `FallbackPolicyEngine`
- `QuotaTracker`
- provider error taxonomy
- provider dashboard

### Required behaviors
- on quota exhaustion, switch automatically
- on rate limit, retry then fallback
- on auth failure, skip or refresh
- persist why a switch occurred
- continue session without operator intervention where possible

- start/stop/restart sessions
- supervise external harnesses
- auto-restart crashed sessions
- expose restart reasons in UI
- show health/live logs
- preserve enough state for continuation

# Canonical config shape

Use JSONC in practice, but here is the canonical structure:

```json
{
  "providers": {
    "policies": {
      "default-coding": {
        "strategy": "quota_aware_capability_first",
        "chain": [
          "anthropic:claude-opus",
          "openai:gpt-5-codex",
          "google:gemini-2.5-pro",
          "openrouter:best_available_coding",
          "local:qwen-coder"
        ],
        "onErrors": {
          "quota_exhausted": "fallback_next",
          "rate_limited": "retry_then_fallback",
          "auth_failed": "skip_provider",
          "provider_down": "fallback_next",
          "timeout": "retry_then_fallback"
        },
        "retry": {
          "maxAttempts": 2,
          "backoffMs": 1500
        },
        "budget": {
          "maxCostUsd": 10
        }
      }
    }
  },
  "sessions": {
    "autoRestart": true,
    "maxRestartsPerHour": 8,
    "crashLoopCooldownMs": 60000
  }
}
```

# Required data contracts

These should be formalized immediately with shared schemas.

## Provider selection result
```ts
type ProviderSelectionResult = {
  providerId: string;
  modelId: string;
  policyId: string;
  reason: string;
  fallbackDepth: number;
  estimatedCost?: number;
  selectedAt: string;
};
```

## Session runtime
```ts
type SessionRuntime = {
  id: string;
  kind: "hypercode-native" | "external-harness" | "mcp-server" | "browser-task";
  harness?: string;
  status: "starting" | "running" | "paused" | "crashed" | "stopped";
  cwd?: string;
  repoPath?: string;
  worktreePath?: string;
  providerPolicyId?: string;
  activeProviderId?: string;
  activeModelId?: string;
  restartCount: number;
  crashLoopDetected: boolean;
  pid?: number;
  startedAt?: string;
  lastHeartbeatAt?: string;
};
```

## Research item
```ts
type ResearchItem = {
  id: string;
  url: string;
  kind: "repo" | "docs" | "issue" | "discussion" | "article" | "concept";
  category?: string;
  title?: string;
  summary?: string;
  relevanceScore?: number;
  integrationDecision?: "submodule" | "native-reimpl" | "wrap-as-plugin" | "index-only" | "reject" | "defer";
  isSubmodule: boolean;
  submodulePath?: string;
  researched: boolean;
  parityTarget: boolean;
};
```

# UI contract: what must be visible

## Mission Control
Must show:

- active session count
- crashed/restarting sessions
- provider currently selected per active session
- CPU/RAM/disk
- MCP/server health summary
- recent important events
- quick actions

## Providers
Must show:

- auth connected/not connected
- quota bars
- reset timers
- fallback chain editor
- provider decision feed
- manual override / auto mode
- per-session routing mode

## Sessions
Must show:

- running/paused/crashed sessions
- harness type
- repo/worktree
- selected provider/model
- restart count
- live logs
- start/stop/restart actions
- broadcast action

## Research
Must show:

- indexed items
- category
- researched/unresearched
- integration decision
- submodule status
- relevance
- parity target status

---

# Hard rule on architecture boundaries

## Main process must stay lean
Do not let it become the place where:
- heavy indexing runs
- browser automation runs
- long-running harness sessions run
- untrusted external wrappers run

The main process should coordinate, persist, expose APIs, and supervise.

---

# Use this runtime rule

## Worker threads for:
- planning
- ranking
- summarization
- compaction
- semantic classification
- research enrichment
- lightweight agent reasoning tasks

## Child processes for:
- external CLI harnesses
- MCP servers
- browser/computer-use runtimes
- sandboxes
- any unstable or long-running autonomous runtime

## Sidecars for:
- OCR
- heavy RAG pipelines
- Python-native ML/document pipelines

That should be the stable rule.

---

# What to stop doing right now

Do not:

- declare new phases complete without repo verification
- keep expanding swarm governance analytics as a priority
- add more submodules without structured research metadata
- tie dashboard architecture to backend router sprawl
- treat external tools as first-class runtime dependencies unless wrapped behind contracts
- confuse “indexed” with “integrated”

---

# Definition of done for Phase 122

A strict real-world gate:

## Provider fallback
- simulated quota exhaustion triggers fallback
- active task continues on fallback model
- decision reason appears in telemetry/UI

## Session supervision
- crashed child process restarts automatically
- crash loop detection prevents infinite respawn
- session appears in Sessions UI with logs and restart reason

## WebUI
- Mission Control renders live system/session state
- Providers panel supports editing fallback policy
- Sessions panel supports start/stop/restart/logs

## Quality
- `pnpm -w typecheck` passes
- `pnpm -w build` passes
- `pnpm run check:dev-readiness` passes

That is a meaningful gate.

## 1. Architecture Consensus (Council Synthesis)
**7-Model Agreement** (GPT-5.x/Gemini/Claude/Kimi/Qwen/Grok): **TypeScript/Node Cellular OS**.
- **Main**: Control Plane (API/tRPC/WS/EventBus).
- **Workers**: Planning/Ranking (isolated v8).
- **Child Procs**: Sessions/MCP/CLIs (crash-safe).
- **No Go/Java**: TS for ecosystem/dashboard unity.
- **MCP**: Interface (Native/Wrapped/Process/MCP modes).
- **Isolation**: Crash=Local Kill + Backoff Restart.

**Runtime Diagram**:
```
Main (Control) ──WS──> Dashboard
                ├──Workers (Agents/Tools)
                └──Child Procs (Sessions/MCP/CLIs)
```

## 4. Dashboard Enhancements (Phase 124 Init: RAG/Memory)
**Operator UX**: Inline `<details>` docs/tooltips everywhere.

### 4.1 Provider Quota Card (LIVE: Consensus Design)
```tsx
// apps/web/src/components/providers/ProviderQuotaCard.tsx
import { api } from '@/utils/trpc';
import { Card, Badge, Progress, Button } from '@/components/ui';
import { Zap, AlertCircle } from 'lucide-react';

export const ProviderQuotaCard = ({ providerId }: { providerId: string }) => {
  const { data: quota } = api.providers.getQuota.useQuery({ id: providerId });
  const connectOAuth = api.providers.connectOAuth.useMutation();

  const pct = (quota?.rpm.used / quota?.rpm.limit || 0) * 100;
  const exhausted = quota?.isExhausted || pct > 90;

  return (
    <Card className={`border ${exhausted ? 'border-red-500' : 'border-green-500'}`}>
      <CardHeader className="flex justify-between items-start">
        <div>
          <h4>{quota?.name}</h4>
          <p className="text-sm text-slate-400">{quota?.model}</p>
        </div>
        {quota?.oauth ? (
          <Badge>✅ Connected</Badge>
        ) : (
          <Button size="sm" onClick={() => connectOAuth.mutate({ providerId })}>Connect OAuth</Button>
        )}
      </CardHeader>
      <CardContent>
        <div className="space-y-2">
          <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
            <span>RPM: {quota?.rpm.used}/{quota?.rpm.limit}</span>
            <span>${quota?.dailyCost.toFixed(2)}/{quota?.budget}</span>
          </div>
          <Progress value={pct} className="h-2" />
          {exhausted && (
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 p-2 bg-red-900/50 rounded">
              <AlertCircle className="h-4 w-4" />
              <span>Exhausted → Fallback Active</span>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
        <details className="mt-2 text-xs text-slate-400">
          <summary>Policy</summary>
          <ul className="ml-4 list-disc">
            <li>429 → Retry 3x → Next</li>
            <li>Quota → Skip + Alert</li>
            <li>Resets: {quota?.resetIn}</li>
          </ul>
        </details>
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
};
```

### 4.2 Session Grid (LIVE: Harness Supervision)
```tsx
// apps/web/src/components/sessions/SessionGrid.tsx (Consensus)
import { api } from '@/utils/trpc';
import { Card, Badge, Button } from '@/components/ui';
import { Play, Pause, RefreshCw } from 'lucide-react';

export const SessionGrid = () => {
  const { data: sessions } = api.sessions.list.useQuery();
  const actions = api.sessions.actions.useMutation();

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
      {sessions?.map((s) => (
        <Card key={s.id} className="h-48">
          <CardHeader>
            <div className="flex justify-between">
              <h5>{s.harness} ({s.dir.split('/').pop()})</h5>
              <Badge variant={s.status === 'running' ? 'default' : 'destructive'}>{s.status}</Badge>
            </div>
          </CardHeader>
          <CardContent className="space-y-3 p-0 h-32 overflow-auto">
            <p>Model: {s.model} | Restarts: {s.count}</p>
            <div className="flex gap-1">
              <Button size="sm" variant="ghost" onClick={() => actions.mutate({ id: s.id, act: 'restart' })}>
                <RefreshCw className="h-3 w-3" />
              </Button>
              <Button size="sm" variant="ghost" onClick={() => actions.mutate({ id: s.id, act: 'pause' })}>
                <Pause className="h-3 w-3" />
              </Button>
              <Button size="sm" variant="ghost" onClick={() => actions.broadcast({ msg: 'Review Plan' })}>
                Broadcast
              </Button>
            </div>
            <details>
              <summary>Policy</summary>
              <ul className="text-xs text-slate-400 ml-4">
                <li>Auto-Restart: Always (Backoff)</li>
                <li>Council: Arch/Guard/Opt</li>
              </ul>
            </details>
          </CardContent>
        </Card>
      ))}
      <Card className="flex items-center justify-center col-span-1 md:col-span-2 xl:col-span-3">
        <Button variant="outline" size="lg" className="w-64">+ New (Opencode/Codex/etc.)</Button>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
};
```
